/**
 * RapidOCR (ONNX Runtime) 集成服务器
 * 专为 4H4G 服务器优化：高准确率、低内存占用、CPU推理快
 *
 * 必需依赖：
 * pip install rapidocr_onnxruntime
 */

const http = require('http');
const { spawn } = require('child_process');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const PORT = 9003;

/**
 * 调用 Python RapidOCR
 * 使用 ONNX Runtime，无需安装完整的 PaddlePaddle，适合轻量级服务器
 */
function recognizeWithPythonOCR(imageBuffer, callback) {
  const imageTempPath = path.join(__dirname, `temp_${Date.now()}.png`);
  fs.writeFileSync(imageTempPath, imageBuffer);

  const pythonScript = `

import sys
import json
import traceback
import os

# 设置环境变量以支持 headless 模式
os.environ['QT_QPA_PLATFORM'] = 'offscreen'
os.environ['DISPLAY'] = ':99'
os.environ['XDG_RUNTIME_DIR'] = '/tmp'
os.environ['MPLBACKEND'] = 'Agg'
os.environ['OPENCV_IO_ENABLE_OPENEXR'] = '0'

# 禁用 GPU 相关功能
os.environ['CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES'] = '-1'
os.environ['TF_CPP_MIN_LOG_LEVEL'] = '2'

try:
    from rapidocr_onnxruntime import RapidOCR

    # 初始化 OCR 引擎 (强制CPU模式)
    # RapidOCR 会自动下载并加载 PP-OCRv4 模型 (高准确率)
    engine = RapidOCR()

    image_path = '${imageTempPath}'

    # 执行识别
    result, elapse = engine(image_path)

    output = []
    if result:
        for item in result:
            # item 结构: [det_box, text, score]
            # det_box 是 [[x1, y1], [x2, y2], [x3, y3], [x4, y4]]
            box = item[0]
            text = item[1]
            score = item[2]

            output.append({
                "box": box,
                "score": score,
                "text": text
            })

    print(json.dumps({"code": 0, "msg": "success", "data": output}, ensure_ascii=False))

except Exception as e:
    # 捕获所有异常并以 JSON 格式输出，方便 Node.js 捕获
    error_msg = str(e) + "\\n" + traceback.format_exc()
    print(json.dumps({"code": 1, "msg": error_msg, "data": []}, ensure_ascii=False))

`;

  const pythonProcess = spawn('python3', ['-c', pythonScript], {
    cwd: __dirname
  });

  let outputData = '';
  let errorData = '';

  pythonProcess.stdout.on('data', (data) => {
    outputData += data.toString();
  });

  pythonProcess.stderr.on('data', (data) => {
    errorData += data.toString();
  });

  pythonProcess.on('close', (code) => {
    // 清理临时文件
    try {
      if (fs.existsSync(imageTempPath)) {
        fs.unlinkSync(imageTempPath);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[OCR Server] 清理临时文件失败:', e);
    }

    if (code !== 0) {
      console.error('[RapidOCR] Python 进程异常退出:', errorData || outputData);
      callback(new Error('OCR 进程异常退出'));
      return;
    }

    try {
      // Python print 的内容可能包含换行符，取最后一行有效的 JSON
      const lines = outputData.trim().split('\n');
      const lastLine = lines[lines.length - 1];
      const result = JSON.parse(lastLine);

      if (result.code !== 0) {
        console.error('[RapidOCR] 内部错误:', result.msg);
        callback(new Error('RapidOCR 识别出错: ' + result.msg));
      } else {
        callback(null, result);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('[RapidOCR] 解析响应失败. 原始内容:', outputData);
      console.error('[RapidOCR] 标准错误输出:', errorData);
      callback(new Error('解析 OCR 响应失败'));
    }
  });
}

/**
 * HTTP服务器请求处理
 */
function parseMultipartRequest(req, callback) {
  const chunks = [];
  req.on('data', (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));
  req.on('end', () => {
    try {
      const buffer = Buffer.concat(chunks);
      const contentType = req.headers['content-type'];
      if (!contentType) return callback(new Error('缺少 Content-Type'));

      const boundaryMatch = contentType.match(/boundary=([^;]+)/);
      if (!boundaryMatch) return callback(new Error('无法找到 boundary'));

      const boundary = boundaryMatch[1].trim();
      const boundaryBuffer = Buffer.from(`--${boundary}`);
      const endBoundaryBuffer = Buffer.from(`--${boundary}--`);

      const result = {};

      let start = 0;
      while (start < buffer.length) {
        // 查找下一个boundary
        const boundaryIndex = buffer.indexOf(boundaryBuffer, start);
        if (boundaryIndex === -1) break;

        // 检查是否是结束boundary
        const endBoundaryIndex = buffer.indexOf(endBoundaryBuffer, start);
        if (endBoundaryIndex !== -1 && endBoundaryIndex < boundaryIndex) {
          break;
        }

        // 移动到boundary之后
        start = boundaryIndex + boundaryBuffer.length;

        // 跳过 \r\n
        if (start + 1 < buffer.length && buffer[start] === 13 && buffer[start + 1] === 10) {
          start += 2;
        } else if (start < buffer.length && buffer[start] === 10) {
          start += 1;
        }

        // 查找头部结束位置
        const headerEndIndex = buffer.indexOf(Buffer.from('\r\n\r\n'), start);
        if (headerEndIndex === -1) continue;

        // 解析头部
        const headers = buffer.slice(start, headerEndIndex).toString();
        const nameMatch = headers.match(/name="([^"]+)"/);
        if (!nameMatch) continue;

        // 获取数据部分
        const dataStart = headerEndIndex + 4;
        const nextBoundaryIndex = buffer.indexOf(boundaryBuffer, dataStart);
        const dataEnd = nextBoundaryIndex !== -1 ? nextBoundaryIndex - 2 : buffer.length; // 减去 \r\n

        if (dataEnd > dataStart) {
          result[nameMatch[1]] = buffer.slice(dataStart, dataEnd);
        }

        start = dataEnd;
      }

      callback(null, result);
    } catch (e) {
      callback(e);
    }
  });
}

function handleOCRRequest(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    res.writeHead(405, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
    res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: '只支持POST方法' }));
    return;
  }

  console.log('[OCR Server] 收到OCR请求');

  parseMultipartRequest(req, (err, formData) => {
    if (err) {
      console.error('[OCR Server] 解析请求失败:', err);
      res.writeHead(400, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
      res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: '解析请求失败', message: err.message }));
      return;
    }

    // 兼容不同的字段名 (image 或 image_file)
    const imageBuffer = formData['image'] || formData['image_file'];

    if (!imageBuffer) {
      res.writeHead(400, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
      res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: '缺少图片数据 (image 或 image_file)' }));
      return;
    }

    console.log(`[OCR Server] 图片大小: ${imageBuffer.length} bytes`);

    recognizeWithPythonOCR(imageBuffer, (error, result) => {
      if (error) {
        res.writeHead(500, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
        res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: 'OCR识别失败', message: error.message }));
      } else {
        console.log(`[OCR Server] 识别完成，返回 ${result.data?.length || 0} 个文本块`);
        res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
        res.end(JSON.stringify(result));
      }
    });
  });
}

function handleHealth(req, res) {
  res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
  res.end(JSON.stringify({ status: 'ok', service: 'RapidOCR Server' }));
}

const server = http.createServer((req, res) => {
  const url = new URL(req.url, `http://${req.headers.host}`);

  // CORS
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, GET, OPTIONS');

  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    res.writeHead(200);
    res.end();
    return;
  }

  if (url.pathname === '/health') {
    handleHealth(req, res);
  } else if (url.pathname === '/ocr') {
    handleOCRRequest(req, res);
  } else {
    res.writeHead(404, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
    res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: '未找到端点' }));
  }
});

server.listen(PORT, '127.0.0.1', () => {
  console.log('========================================');
  console.log('RapidOCR Server (ONNX Runtime)');
  console.log('========================================');
  console.log(`监听地址: http://127.0.0.1:${PORT}`);
  console.log('适用环境: 4H4G 服务器，高准确率，低内存');
  console.log('========================================');
});

  <script>
    // 兼容的 ID 生成函数
    function genId() {
      try {
        if (typeof crypto !== 'undefined' && crypto.randomUUID) {
          return crypto.randomUUID();
        }
        if (typeof globalThis !== 'undefined' && globalThis.crypto && globalThis.crypto.randomUUID) {
          return globalThis.crypto.randomUUID();
        }
      } catch (e) {
        // 降级方案
      }
      // 降级：使用时间戳 + 随机数
      return `id_${Date.now().toString(36)}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`;
    }

    let state = { accounts: [], activeId: "", loginUser: "", loginPassword: "" };
    let saveTimer = null;
    let isLoggedIn = false;
    let pagination = { discordPage: 1, feishuPage: 1, botRelayPage: 1, pageSize: 10 };
    let currentForwardingType = 'discord-to-discord'; // 'discord-to-discord' | 'discord-to-telegram' | 'telegram-to-discord'
    let pendingStatusRender = false;
    let lastFormInteractionAt = 0;
    let isSaving = false;

    function isFormTarget(el) {
      if (!el) return false;
      const tag = el.tagName;
      return tag === 'INPUT' || tag === 'TEXTAREA' || tag === 'SELECT' || el.isContentEditable === true;
    }

    function isFormElementActive() {
      const el = document.activeElement;
      if (el && isFormTarget(el)) return true;
      const form = document.getElementById('configForm');
      if (form && form.matches(':focus-within')) return true;
      return Date.now() - lastFormInteractionAt < 10000;
    }

    function markFormInteraction(target) {
      if (isFormTarget(target)) {
        lastFormInteractionAt = Date.now();
      }
    }

    document.addEventListener('focusin', (event) => markFormInteraction(event.target));
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => markFormInteraction(event.target));
    document.addEventListener('pointerdown', (event) => markFormInteraction(event.target));

    document.addEventListener('focusout', () => {
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (!isFormElementActive() && pendingStatusRender) {
          pendingStatusRender = false;
          render();
        }
      }, 0);
    });

    // 检查登录状态
    function checkLoginStatus() {
      const saved = localStorage.getItem('isLoggedIn');
      return saved === 'true';
    }

    // 设置登录状态
    function setLoginStatus(loggedIn) {
      isLoggedIn = loggedIn;
      localStorage.setItem('isLoggedIn', loggedIn ? 'true' : 'false');
    }

    // 初始化
    async function init() {
      // 检查是否已登录
      if (!checkLoginStatus()) {
        document.getElementById('loginPage').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('mainPage').style.display = 'none';
        return;
      }

      // 已登录，显示主页面
      document.getElementById('loginPage').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('mainPage').style.display = 'block';

      try {
        await loadConfig();
        // 如果没有账号，创建一个默认账号
        if (state.accounts.length === 0) {
          addAccount();
        }
        // 初始化 currentForwardingType
        const activeAccount = state.accounts.find(a => a.id === state.activeId) || state.accounts[0];
        if (activeAccount) {
          currentForwardingType = activeAccount.forwardingType || 'discord-to-discord';
        }
        // 自动检查 Telegram Bot 连接状态
        await autoCheckTelegramBotStatus();
        // 自动检查 Telegram Client 连接状态
        await autoCheckTelegramClientStatus();
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('初始化失败', e);
        // 即使加载失败，也显示界面
        if (state.accounts.length === 0) {
          addAccount();
        }
      } finally {
        document.getElementById('app').style.display = 'block';
        render();
        startStatusPolling();
      }
    }

    // 处理登录
    async function handleLogin() {
      const username = document.getElementById('loginUsername').value.trim();
      const password = document.getElementById('loginPassword').value.trim();
      const errorEl = document.getElementById('loginError');

      if (!username || !password) {
        errorEl.textContent = '请输入用户名和密码';
        errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        return;
      }

      // 加载配置以获取正确的账密
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/config');
        if (!res.ok) {
          errorEl.textContent = '无法连接到服务器';
          errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
          return;
        }
        const data = await res.json();
        const configUser = data.loginUser || 'admin';
        const configPassword = data.loginPassword || 'admin123';

        // 如果配置中账密为空，使用默认值
        const expectedUser = configUser || 'admin';
        const expectedPassword = configPassword || 'admin123';

        if (username === expectedUser && password === expectedPassword) {
          setLoginStatus(true);
          errorEl.classList.add('hidden');
          // 重新初始化以显示主页面
          await init();
        } else {
          errorEl.textContent = '用户名或密码错误';
          errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('登录失败', e);
        errorEl.textContent = '登录失败，请重试';
        errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
      }
    }

    // 处理退出登录
    function handleLogout() {
      if (confirm('确定要退出登录吗？')) {
        setLoginStatus(false);
        document.getElementById('loginPage').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('mainPage').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('app').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('loginUsername').value = '';
        document.getElementById('loginPassword').value = '';
      }
    }

    // 显示修改密码弹窗
    function showChangePasswordModal() {
      const modal = document.getElementById('changePasswordModal');
      if (modal) {
        modal.classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('newUsername').value = state.loginUser || '';
        document.getElementById('newPassword').value = '';
        document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value = '';
        document.getElementById('passwordError').classList.add('hidden');
      }
    }

    // 关闭修改密码弹窗
    function closeChangePasswordModal() {
      const modal = document.getElementById('changePasswordModal');
      if (modal) {
        modal.classList.add('hidden');
      }
    }

    // 保存新密码
    async function saveNewPassword() {
      const newUsername = document.getElementById('newUsername').value.trim();
      const newPassword = document.getElementById('newPassword').value.trim();
      const confirmPassword = document.getElementById('confirmPassword').value.trim();
      const errorEl = document.getElementById('passwordError');

      if (!newUsername) {
        errorEl.textContent = '用户名不能为空';
        errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        return;
      }

      if (newPassword && newPassword !== confirmPassword) {
        errorEl.textContent = '两次输入的密码不一致';
        errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        return;
      }

      // 更新配置
      state.loginUser = newUsername;
      // 如果密码为空，保持原密码不变；否则更新为新密码
      if (newPassword) {
        state.loginPassword = newPassword;
      }

      try {
        // 构建保存的数据
        const saveData = {
          accounts: state.accounts,
          activeId: state.activeId,
          loginUser: state.loginUser,
          telegramAvatarBaseUrl: state.telegramAvatarBaseUrl
        };
        // 只有在新密码不为空时才更新密码
        if (newPassword) {
          saveData.loginPassword = state.loginPassword;
        } else {
          // 如果密码为空，从当前配置中获取原密码
          const res = await fetch('/api/config');
          const data = await res.json();
          saveData.loginPassword = data.loginPassword || state.loginPassword;
        }

        // 直接调用 API 保存配置
        await fetch('/api/config', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify(saveData)
        });
        errorEl.classList.add('hidden');
        closeChangePasswordModal();
        if (newPassword) {
          alert('账密修改成功！请使用新账密重新登录。');
          handleLogout();
        } else {
          alert('用户名修改成功！');
          // 重新加载配置以更新显示
          await loadConfig();
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('保存失败', e);
        errorEl.textContent = '保存失败，请重试';
        errorEl.classList.remove('hidden');
      }
    }

    // 加载配置
    async function loadConfig() {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/config');
        if (!res.ok) {
          console.error('加载配置失败: HTTP', res.status);
          return;
        }
        const data = await res.json();
        console.log('加载配置成功:', data);
        if (Array.isArray(data?.accounts)) {
          // 调试：检查加载的 telegramConfig
          data.accounts.forEach((acc, idx) => {
            if (acc.telegramConfig) {
              console.log(`[DEBUG] 账号 ${idx} 加载的 telegramConfig:`, JSON.stringify(acc.telegramConfig, null, 2));
            }
          });
          state = {
            accounts: data.accounts,
            activeId: data.activeId || data.accounts[0]?.id || "",
            loginUser: data.loginUser || "",
            loginPassword: data.loginPassword || "",
            telegramAvatarBaseUrl: data.telegramAvatarBaseUrl || "",
          };
        } else {
          console.warn('配置数据格式不正确:', data);
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('加载配置失败', e);
        throw e; // 重新抛出错误，让 init 处理
      }
    }

    // 立即保存配置（无防抖，用于关键字段更新）
    async function saveConfigImmediate() {
      isSaving = true;
      try {
        const activeAcc = state.accounts.find(a => a.id === state.activeId);
        if (activeAcc?.telegramConfig) {
          console.log('[DEBUG] 立即保存 telegramConfig:', JSON.stringify(activeAcc.telegramConfig, null, 2));
        }
        const res = await fetch('/api/config', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify(state)
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
          throw new Error(`保存失败: HTTP ${res.status}`);
        }
        console.log('[DEBUG] 立即保存完成');
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('立即保存失败', e);
        alert('保存失败: ' + (e.message || e));
        throw e;
      } finally {
        isSaving = false;
      }
    }

    // 保存配置（防抖）
    async function saveConfig() {
      if (saveTimer) clearTimeout(saveTimer);
      saveTimer = setTimeout(async () => {
        try {
          const activeAcc = state.accounts.find(a => a.id === state.activeId);
          if (activeAcc?.telegramConfig) {
            console.log('[DEBUG] 保存 telegramConfig:', JSON.stringify(activeAcc.telegramConfig, null, 2));
          }
          await fetch('/api/config', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(state)
          });
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('保存失败', e);
        }
      }, 800);
    }

    // 渲染界面
    function render() {
      // 确保 app 元素存在
      const appEl = document.getElementById('app');
      if (!appEl) {
        console.error('找不到 app 元素');
        return;
      }

      if (state.accounts.length === 0) {
        // 如果没有账号，显示提示和添加按钮
        appEl.innerHTML = `
          <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm p-8 text-center">
            <p class="text-slate-400 mb-4">暂无转发实例</p>
            <button onclick="addAccount(); render();" class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-md bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500">
              + 添加转发实例
            </button>
          </div>
        `;
        return;
      }

      const activeAccount = state.accounts.find(a => a.id === state.activeId) || state.accounts[0];
      const resolvedForwardingType = activeAccount.forwardingType || currentForwardingType || 'discord-to-discord';
      if (currentForwardingType !== resolvedForwardingType) {
        currentForwardingType = resolvedForwardingType;
      }
      
      // 渲染账号标签
      // 渲染账号标签
      const accountTabsEl = document.getElementById('accountTabs');
      const configFormEl = document.getElementById('configForm');
      
      if (!accountTabsEl || !configFormEl) {
        console.error('找不到必要的 DOM 元素');
        return;
      }

      let tabsHtml = state.accounts.map(acc => `
        <button onclick="switchAccount('${acc.id}')" 
          class="rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-sm font-medium transition ${
            acc.id === state.activeId 
              ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow' 
              : 'bg-white text-slate-600 border border-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-100'
          }">
          ${acc.name || '未命名账号'}
        </button>
      `).join('');
      tabsHtml += `<button onclick="addAccount(); render();" class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full border border-dashed border-indigo-300 px-3 py-1 text-sm font-medium text-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-50">+ 添加转发实例</button>`;
      accountTabsEl.innerHTML = tabsHtml;

      // 渲染配置表单
      configFormEl.innerHTML = renderAccountForm(activeAccount, currentForwardingType);
    }

    // 渲染账号配置表单
    function renderAccountForm(acc, forwardingType) {
      const isPending = acc.loginState === 'pending';
      const isOnline = acc.loginState === 'online';
      
      return `
        <!-- 基础设置 -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden mb-4">
          <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-100">
            <h2 class="font-semibold text-slate-800">基础设置</h2>
            <p class="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-500">配置转发实例的基本信息和认证凭据</p>
          </div>
          <div class="p-6 space-y-4">
            <div class="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
            <div>
              <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">实例名称</label>
              <input type="text" value="${acc.name || ''}" onchange="updateField('name', this.value)"
                class="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
            </div>
            <div>
              <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">转发类型</label>
              <select onchange="updateField('forwardingType', this.value); updateForwardingUI()"
                class="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
                <option value="discord-to-discord" ${acc.forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' || !acc.forwardingType ? 'selected' : ''}>Discord → Discord</option>
                <option value="discord-to-telegram" ${acc.forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? 'selected' : ''}>Discord → Telegram</option>
                <option value="telegram-to-discord" ${acc.forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? 'selected' : ''}>Telegram → Discord</option>
                <option value="discord-to-feishu" ${acc.forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu' ? 'selected' : ''}>Discord → 飞书</option>
              </select>
            </div>
            </div>

            ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? `
            <!-- Discord→Discord 账号类型选择 -->
            <div class="border-t pt-4 border-slate-200">
              <div>
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">账号类型</label>
                <select onchange="updateField('type', this.value)"
                  class="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
                  <option value="selfbot" ${acc.type === 'selfbot' ? 'selected' : ''}>用户 Token（SelfBot）</option>
                  <option value="bot" ${acc.type === 'bot' ? 'selected' : ''}>机器人 Token</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>
            ` : ''}

            <!-- Discord Token (所有Discord相关类型都需要) -->
            ${(forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' || forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu') ? `
            <div class="border-t pt-4 border-slate-200">
              <div>
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">Discord Token</label>
                <div class="flex gap-2">
                  <input type="password" value="${acc.token || ''}" onchange="updateField('token', this.value)"
                    placeholder="OT..." class="flex-1 px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                  <button onclick="requestLogin()" ${isPending || isOnline ? 'disabled' : ''}
                    class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md ${isPending || isOnline ? 'bg-indigo-300 cursor-not-allowed' : 'bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500'} text-white">
                    ${isPending ? '连接中...' : isOnline ? '已连接' : '连接'}
                  </button>
                  <button onclick="requestStop()" ${isPending || (!isOnline && acc.loginState !== 'error') ? 'disabled' : ''}
                    class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md border border-slate-200 ${isPending || (!isOnline && acc.loginState !== 'error') ? 'cursor-not-allowed bg-slate-50' : 'hover:bg-slate-100'}">
                    断开
                  </button>
                </div>
                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">
                  状态: <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${acc.loginState === 'online' ? 'bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700' : acc.loginState === 'error' ? 'bg-red-50 text-red-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600'}">${acc.loginState || 'idle'}</span>
                  ${acc.loginMessage ? `<span class="ml-2">${acc.loginMessage}</span>` : ''}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            ` : ''}

            ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? `
            <!-- Discord→Telegram Bot配置 -->
            <div class="border-t pt-4 border-slate-200">
              <h3 class="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800 mb-3">Telegram Bot 配置</h3>
              <div>
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">Bot Token</label>
                <div class="flex gap-2">
                  <input type="password" value="${acc.telegramBotToken || ''}" onchange="updateField('telegramBotToken', this.value)"
                    placeholder="从 @BotFather 获取的Token" class="flex-1 px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                  <button onclick="connectTelegramBot()" ${acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting' || acc.telegramBotState === 'online' ? 'disabled' : ''}
                    class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md ${acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting' || acc.telegramBotState === 'online' ? 'bg-indigo-300 cursor-not-allowed' : 'bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500'} text-white">
                    ${acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting' ? '连接中...' : acc.telegramBotState === 'online' ? '已连接' : '连接'}
                  </button>
                  <button onclick="disconnectTelegramBot()" ${acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting' || (acc.telegramBotState !== 'online' && acc.telegramBotState !== 'error') ? 'disabled' : ''}
                    class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md border border-slate-200 ${acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting' || (acc.telegramBotState !== 'online' && acc.telegramBotState !== 'error') ? 'cursor-not-allowed bg-slate-50' : 'hover:bg-slate-100'}">
                    断开
                  </button>
                </div>
                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">
                  状态: <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${acc.telegramBotState === 'online' ? 'bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700' : acc.telegramBotState === 'error' ? 'bg-red-50 text-red-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600'}">${acc.telegramBotState || 'idle'}</span>
                  ${acc.telegramBotMessage ? `<span class="ml-2">${acc.telegramBotMessage}</span>` : ''}
                </div>
                <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">从Telegram的@BotFather获取Bot Token，用于发送消息到Telegram频道</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            ` : forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? `
            <!-- Telegram→Discord Client配置 -->
            <div class="border-t pt-4 border-slate-200">
              <h3 class="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800 mb-3">Telegram Client 配置</h3>
              <div class="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">
                <div>
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">API ID</label>
                  <input type="number" value="${acc.telegramApiId || ''}" onchange="updateField('telegramApiId', this.value)"
                    placeholder="从 https://my.telegram.org 获取" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">API Hash</label>
                  <input type="text" value="${acc.telegramApiHash || ''}" onchange="updateField('telegramApiHash', this.value)"
                    placeholder="从 https://my.telegram.org 获取" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                </div>
              </div>
                <div class="mt-3">
                  <button onclick="toggleFreeApiList()" class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-indigo-600 bg-indigo-50 rounded-lg hover:bg-indigo-100 transition">
                    <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                      <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M12 6V4m0 2a2 2 0 100 4m0-4a2 2 0 110 4m-6 8a2 2 0 100-4m0 4a2 2 0 100 4m0-4v2m0-6V4m6 6v10m6-2a2 2 0 100-4m0 4a2 2 0 100 4m0-4v2m0-6V4"></path>
                    </svg>
                    获取免费API凭据
                  </button>
                  <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">获取预设的免费Telegram API ID和Hash，无需注册</p>
                </div>
                <div id="freeApiSection" class="mt-3 hidden">
                  <div class="bg-slate-50 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                    <div class="flex items-start gap-3 mb-3">
                      <div class="flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-5 bg-blue-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                        <svg class="w-3 h-3 text-blue-600" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20">
                          <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a1 1 0 000 2v3a1 1 0 001 1h1a1 1 0 100-2v-3a1 1 0 00-1-1H9z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path>
                        </svg>
                      </div>
                      <div class="flex-1">
                        <p class="text-sm text-slate-700 font-medium">免费API凭据说明</p>
                        <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">以下是预设的免费Telegram API凭据，可直接使用但可能存在速率限制。如需更好的性能，建议前往 <a href="https://my.telegram.org" target="_blank" class="text-indigo-600 hover:underline">https://my.telegram.org</a> 获取专属凭据。</p>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="space-y-2" id="freeApiList">
                      <!-- 免费API列表将在这里动态生成 -->
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div class="mt-3">
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-2">Session认证</label>
                <div class="border border-slate-200 rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
                  <div class="flex bg-slate-50 border-b border-slate-200">
                    <button onclick="switchSessionType('file')" id="sessionFileTab" class="flex-1 py-2 px-3 text-sm font-medium text-center ${acc.sessionType !== 'string' ? 'bg-white text-indigo-600 border-b-2 border-indigo-600' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-700'}">
                      Session文件
                    </button>
                    <button onclick="switchSessionType('string')" id="sessionStringTab" class="flex-1 py-2 px-3 text-sm font-medium text-center ${acc.sessionType === 'string' ? 'bg-white text-indigo-600 border-b-2 border-indigo-600' : 'text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-700'}">
                      Session字符串
                    </button>
                  </div>
                  <div class="p-3">
                    <div id="sessionFileContent" class="${acc.sessionType === 'string' ? 'hidden' : ''}">
                      <input type="file" accept=".session" onchange="loadSessionFile(this)" class="w-full text-sm text-slate-500 file:mr-4 file:py-2 file:px-4 file:rounded-lg file:border-0 file:text-sm file:font-medium file:bg-indigo-50 file:text-indigo-700 hover:file:bg-indigo-100">
                      <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-2">选择本地的.session文件进行认证</p>
                      ${acc.telegramSessionPath ? `<p class="text-xs text-emerald-600 mt-2">已上传: ${String(acc.telegramSessionPath).split(/[/\\\\]/).pop()}</p>` : ''}
                    </div>
                    <div id="sessionStringContent" class="${acc.sessionType !== 'string' ? 'hidden' : ''}">
                      <textarea onchange="updateField('telegramSessionString', this.value)" rows="3"
                        placeholder="粘贴telethon格式的session字符串..." class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">${acc.telegramSessionString || ''}</textarea>
                      <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-2">粘贴从telethon导出的session字符串</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div class="flex gap-2 mt-3">
                  <button onclick="connectTelegramClient()" ${acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting' || acc.telegramClientState === 'online' ? 'disabled' : ''}
                    class="flex-1 px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium rounded-md ${acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting' || acc.telegramClientState === 'online' ? 'bg-indigo-300 cursor-not-allowed' : 'bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500'} text-white">
                    ${acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting' ? '连接中...' : acc.telegramClientState === 'online' ? '已连接' : '连接'}
                  </button>
                  <button onclick="disconnectTelegramClient()" ${acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting' || (acc.telegramClientState !== 'online' && acc.telegramClientState !== 'error') ? 'disabled' : ''}
                    class="flex-1 px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium rounded-md border border-slate-200 ${acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting' || (acc.telegramClientState !== 'online' && acc.telegramClientState !== 'error') ? 'cursor-not-allowed bg-slate-50' : 'hover:bg-slate-100'}">
                    断开
                  </button>
                </div>
                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-2">
                  状态: <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${acc.telegramClientState === 'online' ? 'bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700' : acc.telegramClientState === 'error' ? 'bg-red-50 text-red-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600'}">${acc.telegramClientState || 'idle'}</span>
                  ${acc.telegramClientMessage ? `<span class="ml-2">${acc.telegramClientMessage}</span>` : ''}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            ` : forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu' ? `
            <!-- Discord→飞书配置 -->
            <div class="border-t pt-4 border-slate-200">
              <h3 class="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800 mb-3">飞书应用配置</h3>
              <div class="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">
                <div>
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">飞书 App ID</label>
                  <input type="text" value="${acc.feishuAppId || ''}" onchange="updateField('feishuAppId', this.value)"
                    placeholder="cli_xxx" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">飞书 App Secret</label>
                  <input type="password" value="${acc.feishuAppSecret || ''}" onchange="updateField('feishuAppSecret', this.value)"
                    placeholder="应用密钥" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                </div>
              </div>
              <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-2">在飞书开发者后台创建企业自建应用，开通 im:resource:upload 和 im:message:send_as_bot 权限</p>
              <p class="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">未填写 AppID/Secret 时只能走 Webhook 文本转发，图片/视频无法转发。</p>
            </div>
            ` : ''}

            <div>
              <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">代理地址</label>
              <input type="text" value="${acc.proxyUrl || ''}" onchange="updateField('proxyUrl', this.value)" 
                placeholder="http://127.0.0.1:7890" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
            </div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.showSourceIdentity ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('showSourceIdentity', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
              <label class="text-sm text-slate-700">
                ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? '使用源用户的昵称进行转发' : '使用源用户的昵称和头像进行转发'}
              </label>
            </div>
            ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? `
            <div class="border-t pt-4 space-y-3">
              <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                <input type="checkbox" ${acc.enableBotRelay ? 'checked' : ''} ${acc.type === 'bot' ? 'disabled' : ''} onchange="updateField('enableBotRelay', this.checked)"
                  class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300 ${acc.type === 'bot' ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">
                <label class="text-sm text-slate-700 ${acc.type === 'bot' ? 'text-slate-400' : ''}">机器人中转（可为不同规则绑定不同的中转机器人）${acc.type === 'bot' ? '（机器人账号类型不支持）' : ''}</label>
              </div>
              ${acc.enableBotRelay && acc.type !== 'bot' ? renderBotRelaySection(acc) : ''}
            </div>
            ` : ''}
              <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                <input type="checkbox" ${acc.enableTranslation ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('enableTranslation', this.checked)" 
                  class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
                <label class="text-sm text-slate-700">启用自动翻译</label>
              </div>
              ${acc.enableTranslation ? `
                <div class="mb-2">
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">翻译服务</label>
                  <select onchange="updateField('translationProvider', this.value)" 
                    class="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
                    <option value="deepseek" ${acc.translationProvider === 'deepseek' || !acc.translationProvider ? 'selected' : ''}>DeepSeek AI</option>
                    <option value="google" ${acc.translationProvider === 'google' ? 'selected' : ''}>Google 翻译</option>
                    <option value="baidu" ${acc.translationProvider === 'baidu' ? 'selected' : ''}>百度翻译</option>
                    <option value="youdao" ${acc.translationProvider === 'youdao' ? 'selected' : ''}>有道智云翻译</option>
                    <option value="openai" ${acc.translationProvider === 'openai' ? 'selected' : ''}>OpenAI</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">API Key / App ID</label>
                  <input type="password" value="${acc.translationApiKey || acc.deepseekApiKey || ''}" onchange="updateField('translationApiKey', this.value)" 
                    placeholder="根据选择的翻译服务填写对应的 API Key" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                </div>
                ${acc.translationProvider === 'baidu' || acc.translationProvider === 'youdao' ? `
                  <div class="mt-2">
                    <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-1">App Secret / Secret Key</label>
                    <input type="password" value="${acc.translationSecret || ''}" onchange="updateField('translationSecret', this.value)" 
                      placeholder="百度/有道智云翻译需要填写 Secret Key" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg focus:outline-none font-mono text-sm">
                  </div>
                ` : ''}
               ` : ''}
              </div>
            </div>

          <!-- 忽略选项 -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden mb-4">
          <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-100">
            <h2 class="font-semibold text-slate-800">忽略选项</h2>
            <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">选择您想要忽略的项目</p>
          </div>
          <div class="p-6">
            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4">
              <label class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.ignoreSelf ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('ignoreSelf', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300"> 忽略自己的消息
              </label>
              <label class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.ignoreBot ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('ignoreBot', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300"> 忽略机器人消息
              </label>
              <label class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.ignoreImages ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('ignoreImages', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300"> 忽略图片
              </label>
              <label class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.ignoreAudio ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('ignoreAudio', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300"> 忽略音频
              </label>
              <label class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.ignoreVideo ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('ignoreVideo', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300"> 忽略视频
              </label>
              <label class="inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
              <input type="checkbox" ${acc.ignoreDocuments ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('ignoreDocuments', this.checked)" 
                class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300"> 忽略文档
              </label>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 转发规则 -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden mb-4">
          <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-100">
            <h2 class="font-semibold text-slate-800">
              ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? 'Discord 转发规则' :
                forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? 'Discord → Telegram 转发规则' :
                forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? 'Telegram → Discord 转发规则' :
                'Discord → 飞书 转发规则'}
            </h2>
            <p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-1">
              ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? '配置Discord频道之间的转发映射关系' :
                forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? '配置Discord消息转发到Telegram频道的映射关系' :
                forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? '配置Telegram消息转发到Discord频道的映射关系' :
                '配置Discord消息转发到飞书的映射关系'}
            </p>
          </div>


          <div class="p-6 space-y-6" id="mappingsList">
            ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? `
            <!-- Discord→Discord 转发规则 -->
            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 mb-4">
              <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">Discord 转发样式：</span>
              <select onchange="updateField('feishuStyle', this.value)"
                class="rounded border border-slate-200 px-2 py-1 text-xs focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
                <option value="style1" ${acc.feishuStyle === 'style2' ? '' : 'selected'}>样式1：内嵌</option>
                <option value="style2" ${acc.feishuStyle === 'style2' ? 'selected' : ''}>样式2：文本+时间</option>
              </select>
            </div>
            <div class="space-y-3 ${acc.enableDiscordForward !== false ? '' : 'opacity-60'}">
              <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <input type="checkbox" ${acc.enableDiscordForward !== false ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('enableDiscordForward', this.checked)" class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
                  <span class="text-sm text-slate-800 font-medium">Discord 转发规则</span>
                </div>
                ${acc.enableDiscordForward !== false ? `<button onclick="addMapping()" class="text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-indigo-100">+ 添加规则</button>` : ''}
              </div>
              ${acc.enableDiscordForward !== false ? renderMappings(acc, forwardingType) : '<div class="text-slate-400 text-sm">已关闭 Discord 转发</div>'}
            </div>
            <div class="border-t pt-4 space-y-3 ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? '' : 'opacity-60'}">
              <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                  <input type="checkbox" ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('enableFeishuForward', this.checked)" class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
                  <span class="text-sm text-slate-800 font-medium">飞书转发规则</span>
                </div>
                ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? `<button onclick="addFeishuMapping()" class="text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-indigo-100">+ 添加规则</button>` : ''}
              </div>
              ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? `
                <div class="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2 items-end">
                  <div>
                    <label class="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-600 mb-1">飞书 App ID</label>
                    <input type="text" value="${acc.feishuAppId || ''}" onchange="updateField('feishuAppId', this.value)"
                      placeholder="cli_xxx" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-xs font-mono">
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <label class="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-600 mb-1">飞书 App Secret</label>
                    <input type="password" value="${acc.feishuAppSecret || ''}" onchange="updateField('feishuAppSecret', this.value)"
                      placeholder="应用密钥，建议勿泄露" class="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-xs font-mono">
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div class="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">未填写 AppID/Secret 时只能通过 Webhook 文本转发，图片/视频无法转发。</div>
                <div id="feishuChats" class="mt-2 text-xs text-slate-500"></div>
                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 bg-slate-50 border border-dashed border-slate-200 rounded-md p-3 space-y-1">
                  <p>Webhook：填写飞书自定义机器人 Webhook 地址。</p>
                  <p>话题 Thread：填写 thread_id（话题根消息 message_id）。获取方式：订阅 <code class="px-1 bg-slate-100 rounded">im.message.receive_v1</code> 事件保存 message_id，或用历史消息接口找到 root_id 为空的 message_id。可为不同 Discord 频道配置不同 thread_id。</p>
                </div>
                ${renderFeishuMappings(acc)}
              ` : '<div class="text-slate-400 text-sm">未启用飞书转发</div>'}
            </div>
            ` : forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? `
            <!-- Discord→Telegram 转发规则 -->
            <div class="space-y-3">
              <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <input type="checkbox" ${isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateTelegramForwarding(this.checked)" class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
                  <span class="text-sm text-slate-800 font-medium">Discord → Telegram 转发规则</span>
                </div>
                ${isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) ? `<button onclick="addMapping()" class="text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-indigo-100">+ 添加规则</button>` : ''}
              </div>
              ${isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) ? renderMappings(acc, forwardingType) : '<div class="text-slate-400 text-sm">已关闭 Discord→Telegram 转发</div>'}
            </div>
            ` : forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? `
            <!-- Telegram→Discord 转发规则 -->
            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 mb-4">
              <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">转发样式：</span>
              <select onchange="updateField('feishuStyle', this.value)"
                class="rounded border border-slate-200 px-2 py-1 text-xs focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
                <option value="style1" ${acc.feishuStyle === 'style2' ? '' : 'selected'}>样式1：内嵌</option>
                <option value="style2" ${acc.feishuStyle === 'style2' ? 'selected' : ''}>样式2：文本+时间</option>
              </select>
            </div>
            <div class="space-y-3">
              <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <input type="checkbox" ${isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateTelegramForwarding(this.checked)" class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
                  <span class="text-sm text-slate-800 font-medium">Telegram → Discord 转发规则</span>
                </div>
                ${isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) ? `<button onclick="addMapping()" class="text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-indigo-100">+ 添加规则</button>` : ''}
              </div>
              ${isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) ? renderMappings(acc, forwardingType) : '<div class="text-slate-400 text-sm">已关闭 Telegram→Discord 转发</div>'}
            </div>
            ` : forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu' ? `
            <!-- Discord→飞书 转发规则 -->
            <div class="space-y-3">
              <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                  <input type="checkbox" ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="updateField('enableFeishuForward', this.checked)" class="h-4 w-4 rounded border-slate-300">
                  <span class="text-sm text-slate-800 font-medium">飞书转发规则</span>
                </div>
                ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? `<button onclick="addFeishuMapping()" class="text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-indigo-100">+ 添加规则</button>` : ''}
              </div>
              ${acc.enableFeishuForward ? `
                <div id="feishuChats" class="mt-2 text-xs text-slate-500"></div>
                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 bg-slate-50 border border-dashed border-slate-200 rounded-md p-3 space-y-1">
                  <p>Webhook：填写飞书自定义机器人 Webhook 地址。</p>
                  <p>话题 Thread：填写 thread_id（话题根消息 message_id）。获取方式：订阅 <code class="px-1 bg-slate-100 rounded">im.message.receive_v1</code> 事件保存 message_id，或用历史消息接口找到 root_id 为空的 message_id。可为不同 Discord 频道配置不同 thread_id。</p>
                </div>
                ${renderFeishuMappings(acc)}
              ` : '<div class="text-slate-400 text-sm">未启用飞书转发</div>'}
            </div>
            ` : ''}
          </div>
        </div>


        <!-- 关键词过滤 -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden mb-4">
          <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-100">
            <h2 class="font-semibold text-slate-800">关键词触发（至少命中一个才转发）</h2>
          </div>
          <div class="p-6">
            <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
              ${(acc.blockedKeywords || []).map(k => `
                <span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full bg-red-50 text-red-600 text-sm border border-red-100">
                  ${k} <button onclick="removeKeyword('blockedKeywords', '${k}')" class="hover:text-red-800">✕</button>
                </span>
              `).join('')}
              <input type="text" placeholder="输入关键词后回车..." onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter') handleKeywordEnter(this, 'blockedKeywords')"
                class="flex-1 min-w-[120px] px-3 py-1 border-none focus:outline-none text-sm">
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 排除关键词 -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden mb-4">
          <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-100">
            <h2 class="font-semibold text-slate-800">屏蔽关键词（命中则不转发）</h2>
          </div>
          <div class="p-6">
            <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
              ${(acc.excludeKeywords || []).map(k => `
                <span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full bg-amber-50 text-amber-700 text-sm border border-amber-100">
                  ${k} <button onclick="removeKeyword('excludeKeywords', '${k}')" class="hover:text-amber-900">✕</button>
                </span>
              `).join('')}
              <input type="text" placeholder="输入屏蔽词后回车..." onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter') handleKeywordEnter(this, 'excludeKeywords')"
                class="flex-1 min-w-[120px] px-3 py-1 border-none focus:outline-none text-sm">
            </div>
            <div class="border-t pt-4">
              <div class="mb-4">
                <label class="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700 mb-3">OCR 屏蔽关键词（检测到这些词的图片不会转发）</label>
                <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                  ${(acc.ocrBlockedKeywords || []).map(k => `
                    <span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full bg-amber-50 text-amber-700 text-sm border border-amber-100">
                      ${k} <button onclick="removeOCRKeyword('ocrBlockedKeywords', '${k}')" class="hover:text-amber-900">✕</button>
                    </span>
                  `).join('')}
                  <input type="text" placeholder="输入屏蔽词后回车..." onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter') handleKeywordEnter(this, 'ocrBlockedKeywords', true)"
                    class="flex-1 min-w-[120px] px-3 py-1 border-none focus:outline-none text-sm">
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 替换规则 -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-slate-200 shadow-sm overflow-hidden mb-4">
          <div class="px-6 py-4 border-b border-slate-100">
            <h2 class="font-semibold text-slate-800">关键词替换</h2>
          </div>
          <div class="p-6 space-y-2" id="replacementsList">
            ${renderReplacements(acc.replacements || [])}
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
    }

    function updateGlobal(field, value) {
      if (!state) return;
      state[field] = value;
      saveConfig();
    }

    function renderMappings(acc, forwardingType) {
      // 根据转发类型决定读取哪个数组
      const mappings = (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord')
        ? (acc.telegramConfig?.mappings || [])
        : (acc.mappings || []);
      console.log('[DEBUG] renderMappings - mappings长度:', mappings.length);
      console.log('[DEBUG] renderMappings - 当前页:', pagination.discordPage);
      console.log('[DEBUG] renderMappings - 第一个mapping ID:', mappings[0]?.id);

      const { discordPage, pageSize } = pagination;
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(mappings.length / pageSize) || 1;
      const startIdx = (discordPage - 1) * pageSize;
      const endIdx = startIdx + pageSize;
      const currentPageMappings = mappings.slice(startIdx, endIdx);

      console.log('[DEBUG] renderMappings - 当前页显示数量:', currentPageMappings.length);

      if (mappings.length === 0) {
        const typeName = forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? 'Discord' :
                        forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? 'Discord→Telegram' :
                        forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? 'Telegram→Discord' :
                        'Discord→飞书';
        return `<div class="text-center py-8 text-slate-400 text-sm">暂无 ${typeName} 规则，点击"添加规则"创建</div>`;
      }

      const mappingsHtml = currentPageMappings.map((m, idx) => {
        let sourcePlaceholder = '来源频道 ID';
        let targetPlaceholder = '目标频道 ID';
        let arrowIcon = '→';

        if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord') {
          sourcePlaceholder = 'Discord 频道 ID';
          targetPlaceholder = 'Discord Webhook URL';
          arrowIcon = '→';
        } else if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram') {
          sourcePlaceholder = 'Discord 频道 ID';
          targetPlaceholder = 'Telegram 频道/Chat ID';
          arrowIcon = '→';
        } else if (forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
          sourcePlaceholder = 'Telegram 频道/Chat ID';
          targetPlaceholder = 'Discord Webhook URL';
          arrowIcon = '→';
        } else if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu') {
          sourcePlaceholder = 'Discord 频道 ID';
          targetPlaceholder = '飞书 Webhook 地址';
          arrowIcon = '→';
        }

        return `
        <div class="flex flex-col gap-2 p-3 rounded-lg border border-slate-100 bg-slate-50/30">
          <div class="flex gap-3 items-center flex-wrap">
            <input type="text" value="${m.sourceChannelId || ''}" onchange="updateMapping(${idx + startIdx}, 'sourceChannelId', this.value)"
              placeholder="${sourcePlaceholder}" class="w-48 px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
            <span class="text-slate-300">${arrowIcon}</span>
            <input type="text" value="${m.targetChannelId || m.targetWebhookUrl || ''}" onchange="updateMapping(${idx + startIdx}, '${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? 'targetWebhookUrl' : forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu' ? 'targetChannelId' : 'targetChannelId'}', this.value)"
              placeholder="${targetPlaceholder}" class="flex-1 px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
            ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-discord' ? `
            <select onchange="updateMappingRelay(${idx + startIdx}, this.value)" class="w-44 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-200 text-sm focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
              <option value="">Webhook 默认</option>
              ${(acc.botRelays || []).map(r => `<option value="${r.id}" ${acc.channelRelayMap?.[m.sourceChannelId || ''] === r.id ? 'selected' : ''}>${r.name || '中转机器人'}</option>`).join('')}
            </select>
            ` : ''}
            <input type="text" value="${m.note || ''}" onchange="updateMapping(${idx + startIdx}, 'note', this.value)"
              placeholder="备注" class="w-32 px-3 py-1.5 border border-dashed border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-xs focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none">
            <select onchange="updateMapping(${idx + startIdx}, 'translateDirection', this.value)"
              ${!acc.enableTranslation ? 'disabled' : ''}
              class="px-2 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none ${!acc.enableTranslation ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">
              <option value="off" ${(!acc.enableTranslation || m.translateDirection === 'off' || (!m.translateDirection && !acc.enableTranslation)) ? 'selected' : ''}>关闭翻译</option>
              <option value="auto" ${(acc.enableTranslation && (m.translateDirection === 'auto' || (!m.translateDirection && acc.enableTranslation))) ? 'selected' : ''}>自动检测</option>
              <option value="zh-en" ${m.translateDirection === 'zh-en' ? 'selected' : ''}>中 → 英</option>
              <option value="en-zh" ${m.translateDirection === 'en-zh' ? 'selected' : ''}>英 → 中</option>
            </select>
            ${forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' ? `
            <button onclick="openLongMessageConfigModal(${idx + startIdx}, '${forwardingType}')" class="p-1.5 text-slate-400 hover:text-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-50 rounded" title="超长消息处理配置">
              ⚙️
            </button>
            ` : ''}
            <button onclick="removeMapping(${idx + startIdx})" class="p-2 text-slate-400 hover:text-red-500 rounded hover:bg-red-50">删除</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      `}).join('');

      const paginationHtml = totalPages > 1 ? `
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-slate-200">
          <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">共 ${mappings.length} 条规则</span>
          <div class="flex gap-2">
            <button onclick="goToDiscordPage(1)" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${discordPage === 1 ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">首页</button>
            <button onclick="goToDiscordPage(${discordPage - 1})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${discordPage === 1 ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">上一页</button>
            <span class="px-3 py-1 text-xs text-slate-700 bg-slate-100 rounded">${discordPage} / ${totalPages}</span>
            <button onclick="goToDiscordPage(${discordPage + 1})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${discordPage >= totalPages ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">下一页</button>
            <button onclick="goToDiscordPage(${totalPages})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${discordPage >= totalPages ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">尾页</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      ` : '';

      return mappingsHtml + paginationHtml;
    }

    function renderFeishuMappings(acc) {
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const { feishuPage, pageSize } = pagination;
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(entries.length / pageSize) || 1;
      const startIdx = (feishuPage - 1) * pageSize;
      const endIdx = startIdx + pageSize;
      const currentPageEntries = entries.slice(startIdx, endIdx);

      if (entries.length === 0) {
        return '<div class="text-center py-8 text-slate-400 text-sm">暂无飞书规则，点击"添加规则"创建</div>';
      }

      const entriesHtml = currentPageEntries.map((m, idx) => `
        <div class="flex flex-col gap-2 p-3 rounded-lg border border-slate-100 bg-slate-50/30">
          <div class="flex gap-3 items-center flex-wrap">
            <input type="text" value="${(m.sourceChannelId || '').startsWith('new_') ? '' : (m.sourceChannelId || '')}" onchange="updateFeishuSource(${idx + startIdx}, this.value)"
              placeholder="Discord 频道 ID" class="w-48 px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono">
            <span class="text-slate-300">→</span>
            <select onchange="updateFeishuMode(${idx + startIdx}, this.value)"
              class="px-2 py-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-200 text-sm">
              <option value="webhook" ${m.mode === 'thread' ? '' : 'selected'}>Webhook</option>
              <option value="thread" ${m.mode === 'thread' ? 'selected' : ''}>话题 Thread</option>
            </select>
            ${m.mode === 'thread' ? `
              <input type="text" value="${m.threadId || ''}" onchange="updateFeishuThreadId(${idx + startIdx}, this.value)"
                placeholder="话题 Thread ID (root_id)" class="flex-1 min-w-[220px] px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono">
            ` : `
              <input type="text" value="${m.webhookUrl || ''}" onchange="updateFeishuWebhookEntry(${idx + startIdx}, this.value)"
                placeholder="飞书 Webhook 地址" class="flex-1 min-w-[260px] px-3 py-2 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono">
            `}
            <input type="text" value="${m.note || ''}" onchange="updateFeishuNote(${idx + startIdx}, this.value)"
              placeholder="备注" class="w-32 px-3 py-1.5 border border-dashed border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-xs">
            <button onclick="removeFeishuMapping(${idx + startIdx})" class="p-2 text-slate-400 hover:text-red-500">删除</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      `).join('');

      const paginationHtml = totalPages > 1 ? `
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-slate-200">
          <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">共 ${entries.length} 条规则</span>
          <div class="flex gap-2">
            <button onclick="goToFeishuPage(1)" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${feishuPage === 1 ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">首页</button>
            <button onclick="goToFeishuPage(${feishuPage - 1})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${feishuPage === 1 ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">上一页</button>
            <span class="px-3 py-1 text-xs text-slate-700 bg-slate-100 rounded">${feishuPage} / ${totalPages}</span>
            <button onclick="goToFeishuPage(${feishuPage + 1})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${feishuPage >= totalPages ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">下一页</button>
            <button onclick="goToFeishuPage(${totalPages})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${feishuPage >= totalPages ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">尾页</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      ` : '';

      return entriesHtml + paginationHtml;
    }

    function normalizeFeishuTargetValue(raw) {
      if (typeof raw === 'string') {
        return { mode: 'webhook', webhookUrl: raw, threadId: '' };
      }
      if (!raw || typeof raw !== 'object') {
        return { mode: 'webhook', webhookUrl: '', threadId: '' };
      }
      const mode = raw.mode === 'thread' ? 'thread' : 'webhook';
      return {
        mode,
        webhookUrl: raw.webhookUrl || '',
        threadId: raw.threadId || '',
      };
    }

    function getFeishuMappings(acc) {
      const hooks = acc.channelFeishuWebhooks || {};
      const notes = acc.channelNotes || {};

      // 将entries转换为数组，并按照特定顺序排序
      const entries = Object.entries(hooks);

      // 排序规则：以'new_'开头的key排在前面，然后是其他key
      entries.sort(([a], [b]) => {
        const aIsNew = a.startsWith('new_');
        const bIsNew = b.startsWith('new_');
        if (aIsNew && !bIsNew) return -1;
        if (!aIsNew && bIsNew) return 1;
        return 0; // 保持其他相对顺序
      });

      return entries.map(([source, raw]) => {
        const target = normalizeFeishuTargetValue(raw);
        return {
          sourceChannelId: source,
          mode: target.mode,
          webhookUrl: target.webhookUrl,
          threadId: target.threadId,
          note: notes[source] || ''
        };
      });
    }

    function toggleFeishuHelp() {
      const el = document.getElementById('feishuHelp');
      if (!el) return;
      el.classList.toggle('hidden');
    }
