    function toggleFreeApiList() {
      const section = document.getElementById('freeApiSection');
      const isHidden = section.classList.contains('hidden');

      if (isHidden) {
        // 展开时生成列表
        generateFreeApiList();
        section.classList.remove('hidden');
      } else {
        // 折叠
        section.classList.add('hidden');
      }
    }

    function generateFreeApiList() {
      const listEl = document.getElementById('freeApiList');
      listEl.innerHTML = freeApis.map(api => `
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-white border border-slate-200 rounded-lg">
          <div class="flex-1">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-4">
              <div class="text-sm">
                <span class="font-medium text-slate-700">API ID:</span>
                <code class="px-2 py-0.5 bg-slate-100 rounded text-xs font-mono">${api.apiId}</code>
              </div>
              <div class="text-sm">
                <span class="font-medium text-slate-700">API Hash:</span>
                <code class="px-2 py-0.5 bg-slate-100 rounded text-xs font-mono">${api.apiHash}</code>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="flex gap-2">
            <button onclick="copyToClipboard('${api.apiId}', 'API ID')" class="px-3 py-1 text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 rounded hover:bg-indigo-100 transition">
              复制ID
            </button>
            <button onclick="copyToClipboard('${api.apiHash}', 'API Hash')" class="px-3 py-1 text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 rounded hover:bg-indigo-100 transition">
              复制Hash
            </button>
            <button onclick="useApiCredentials('${api.apiId}', '${api.apiHash}')" class="px-3 py-1 text-xs bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-600 rounded hover:bg-emerald-100 transition">
              使用此凭据
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      `).join('');
    }

    function copyToClipboard(text, type) {
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => {
        // 显示临时成功提示
        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.className = 'fixed top-4 right-4 bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50';
        notification.textContent = `${type}已复制到剪贴板`;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);

        setTimeout(() => {
          document.body.removeChild(notification);
        }, 2000);
      }).catch(err => {
        console.error('复制失败:', err);
        // 降级到传统方法
        const textArea = document.createElement('textarea');
        textArea.value = text;
        document.body.appendChild(textArea);
        textArea.select();
        document.execCommand('copy');
        document.body.removeChild(textArea);

        const notification = document.createElement('div');
        notification.className = 'fixed top-4 right-4 bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50';
        notification.textContent = `${type}已复制到剪贴板`;
        document.body.appendChild(notification);

        setTimeout(() => {
          document.body.removeChild(notification);
        }, 2000);
      });
    }

    function useApiCredentials(apiId, apiHash) {
      // 自动填充API ID和Hash输入框
      const apiIdInput = document.querySelector('input[onchange*="telegramApiId"]');
      const apiHashInput = document.querySelector('input[onchange*="telegramApiHash"]');

      if (apiIdInput) apiIdInput.value = apiId;
      if (apiHashInput) apiHashInput.value = apiHash;

      // 触发change事件以更新配置
      if (apiIdInput) apiIdInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));
      if (apiHashInput) apiHashInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));

      // 显示成功提示
      const notification = document.createElement('div');
      notification.className = 'fixed top-4 right-4 bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50';
      notification.textContent = 'API凭据已自动填写';
      document.body.appendChild(notification);

      setTimeout(() => {
        document.body.removeChild(notification);
      }, 2000);
    }

      async function fetchFeishuChats() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.id) return;
      const container = document.getElementById('feishuChats');
      if (container) {
        container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-xs text-slate-500">正在从飞书获取群列表...</div>';
      }
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/feishu/chats', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id }),
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (!res.ok) {
          throw new Error(data?.error || `请求失败(${res.status})`);
        }
        const items = Array.isArray(data.items) ? data.items : [];
        if (container) {
          if (items.length === 0) {
            container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-xs text-slate-500">未获取到任何群，请确认机器人已被拉入群并具有权限。</div>';
          } else {
            container.innerHTML = `
              <div class="mt-2 max-h-40 overflow-auto rounded border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50/60 p-2 text-xs text-slate-700 space-y-1">
                ${items
                  .map(
                    (it) => `
                  <div class="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
                    <div class="min-w-0">
                      <div class="truncate font-medium">${it.name || '未命名群'}</div>
                      <div class="truncate font-mono text-[11px] text-slate-500">${it.chat_id || ''}</div>
                    </div>
                    <button type="button" onclick="navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText('${it.chat_id || ''}')" class="shrink-0 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-slate-200 text-[11px] text-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-100">复制</button>
                  </div>
                `,
                  )
                  .join('')}
              </div>
              <div class="mt-1 text-[11px] text-slate-400">
                提示：若使用 AppID/Secret + Chat ID，请将上方 Chat ID（<code class="px-1 bg-slate-100 rounded">oc_...</code>）填入对应规则的“飞书 Webhook 地址”；使用 Webhook 时可忽略本列表。
                <a href="https://open.feishu.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="ml-1 text-indigo-500 hover:underline">打开飞书开放平台</a>
              </div>
            `;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        if (container) {
          var msg = (e && e.message) ? e.message : e;
          container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-xs text-red-500">获取失败：' + msg + '</div>';
        }
      }
    }

    function renderReplacements(replacements) {
      return replacements.map((r, idx) => `
        <div class="flex gap-2 items-center">
          <input type="text" value="${r.from || ''}" oninput="updateReplacement(${idx}, 'from', this.value)" 
            placeholder="原词" class="w-40 px-3 py-1.5 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono">
          <span class="text-slate-400">→</span>
          <input type="text" value="${r.to || ''}" oninput="updateReplacement(${idx}, 'to', this.value)" 
            placeholder="替换为" class="flex-1 px-3 py-1.5 border border-slate-200 rounded-lg text-sm font-mono">
          <button onclick="removeReplacement(${idx})" class="p-2 text-slate-400 hover:text-red-500">删除</button>
        </div>
      `).join('') + '<button onclick="addReplacement()" class="text-xs bg-slate-50 text-slate-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-md hover:bg-slate-100 mt-2">+ 添加替换规则</button>';
    }

    function renderBotRelaySection(acc) {
      const relays = acc.botRelays || [];
      const { botRelayPage, pageSize } = pagination;
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(relays.length / pageSize) || 1;
      const startIdx = (botRelayPage - 1) * pageSize;
      const endIdx = startIdx + pageSize;
      const currentPageRelays = relays.slice(startIdx, endIdx);

      const paginationHtml = totalPages > 1 ? `
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-slate-200">
          <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">共 ${relays.length} 个中转机器人</span>
          <div class="flex gap-2">
            <button onclick="goToBotRelayPage(1)" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${botRelayPage === 1 ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">首页</button>
            <button onclick="goToBotRelayPage(${botRelayPage - 1})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${botRelayPage === 1 ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">上一页</button>
            <span class="px-3 py-1 text-xs text-slate-700 bg-slate-100 rounded">${botRelayPage} / ${totalPages}</span>
            <button onclick="goToBotRelayPage(${botRelayPage + 1})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${botRelayPage >= totalPages ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">下一页</button>
            <button onclick="goToBotRelayPage(${totalPages})" class="px-3 py-1 rounded border border-slate-200 text-xs hover:bg-slate-100 ${botRelayPage >= totalPages ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}">尾页</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      ` : '';

      return `
        <div class="mb-4 rounded-lg border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50/60 p-3 space-y-3">
          <div class="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div class="text-sm text-slate-700">配置多个中转机器人，稍后在每条转发规则中选择要使用的机器人。</div>
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
              <button onclick="requestRelayLoginAll()" class="text-xs bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-600 px-2 py-1 rounded-md hover:bg-emerald-100">一键登录</button>
              <button onclick="requestRelayStopAll()" class="text-xs bg-slate-100 text-slate-600 px-2 py-1 rounded-md hover:bg-slate-200">一键停止</button>
              <button onclick="addBotRelay()" class="text-xs bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600 px-2 py-1 rounded-md hover:bg-indigo-100">+ 添加中转机器人</button>
            </div>
          </div>
          ${relays.length === 0 ? `<div class="text-sm text-slate-400">暂无中转机器人，请点击"添加"创建。</div>` : currentPageRelays.map((r, idx) => `
            <div class="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-[1fr,1fr,auto] items-center border border-slate-200 rounded-lg p-3">
              <div>
                <label class="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-600 mb-1">名称</label>
                <input type="text" value="${r.name || ''}" onchange="updateBotRelay(${idx + startIdx}, 'name', this.value)"
                  class="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none" placeholder="例如：Relay-1">
              </div>
              <div>
                <label class="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-600 mb-1">机器人 Token</label>
                <input type="password" value="${r.token || ''}" onchange="updateBotRelay(${idx + startIdx}, 'token', this.value)"
                  class="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 px-3 py-2 font-mono focus:border-indigo-500 focus:outline-none" placeholder="机器人 Token">
              </div>
              <div class="flex flex-col items-end justify-center gap-2 pt-5 md:pt-0">
                <div class="text-xs">
                  <span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${r.loginState === 'online' ? 'bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-700' : r.loginState === 'error' ? 'bg-red-50 text-red-700' : r.loginState === 'pending' ? 'bg-amber-50 text-amber-700' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600'}">${r.loginState || 'idle'}</span>
                  ${r.loginMessage ? `<span class="ml-1 text-slate-500">${r.loginMessage}</span>` : ''}
                </div>
                <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <button onclick="requestRelayLogin('${r.id}')" ${r.loginState === 'pending' || r.loginState === 'online' ? 'disabled' : ''} class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md border border-slate-200 ${r.loginState === 'pending' || r.loginState === 'online' ? 'cursor-not-allowed bg-slate-50' : 'hover:bg-slate-100'} text-slate-600">登录</button>
                  <button onclick="requestRelayStop('${r.id}')" class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md border border-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-100 text-slate-600">停止</button>
                  <button onclick="removeBotRelay(${idx + startIdx})" class="px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-md border border-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-100 text-slate-600">删除</button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          `).join('')}
          ${paginationHtml}
        </div>
      `;
    }

    // 工具函数
    function getActiveAccount() {
      return state.accounts.find(a => a.id === state.activeId) || state.accounts[0];
    }

    function ensureTelegramConfig(acc) {
      if (!acc.telegramConfig) {
        acc.telegramConfig = { accounts: [], mappings: [], enableTelegramForward: true };
      }
      if (!acc.telegramConfig.accounts) acc.telegramConfig.accounts = [];
      if (!acc.telegramConfig.mappings) acc.telegramConfig.mappings = [];
      if (acc.telegramConfig.enableTelegramForward === undefined) {
        acc.telegramConfig.enableTelegramForward = acc.enableForwarding !== false;
      }
    }

    function isTelegramForwardEnabled(acc) {
      if (!acc.telegramConfig) return acc.enableForwarding !== false;
      if (acc.telegramConfig.enableTelegramForward === undefined) {
        return acc.enableForwarding !== false;
      }
      return acc.telegramConfig.enableTelegramForward !== false;
    }

    function updateTelegramForwarding(enabled) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      ensureTelegramConfig(acc);
      acc.telegramConfig.enableTelegramForward = enabled;
      acc.enableForwarding = enabled;
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateField(field, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      acc[field] = value;
      // 当启用自动翻译时，自动将所有频道的翻译方向设为"自动检测"
      if (field === 'enableTranslation' && value === true) {
        if (!acc.channelTranslateDirection) acc.channelTranslateDirection = {};
        if (acc.mappings) {
          acc.mappings.forEach(m => {
            if (m.sourceChannelId) {
              acc.channelTranslateDirection[m.sourceChannelId] = 'auto';
            }
          });
        }
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateTelegramLongMessage(field, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.telegramLongMessage) acc.telegramLongMessage = { enabled: false };

      if (field === 'enabled') {
        acc.telegramLongMessage.enabled = value;
        if (!value) {
          // 禁用时清空其他设置
          acc.telegramLongMessage.threshold = undefined;
          acc.telegramLongMessage.appendMessage = undefined;
        }
      } else if (field === 'threshold') {
        const numeric = typeof value === 'number' ? value : parseInt(value, 10);
        acc.telegramLongMessage.threshold = Number.isFinite(numeric) ? numeric : undefined;
      } else if (field === 'appendMessage') {
        acc.telegramLongMessage.appendMessage = value || undefined;
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateMappingLongMessage(mappingIndex, field, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();

      // 根据转发类型获取正确的映射配置
      let mapping;
      if (currentLongMessageForwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || currentLongMessageForwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
        if (!acc.telegramConfig) acc.telegramConfig = {};
        if (!acc.telegramConfig.mappings) acc.telegramConfig.mappings = [];
        if (!acc.telegramConfig.mappings[mappingIndex]) return;
        mapping = acc.telegramConfig.mappings[mappingIndex];
      } else {
        if (!acc.mappings) acc.mappings = [];
        if (!acc.mappings[mappingIndex]) return;
        mapping = acc.mappings[mappingIndex];
      }

      if (!mapping.longMessage) mapping.longMessage = { enabled: false };

      if (field === 'enabled') {
        mapping.longMessage.enabled = value;
        if (!value) {
          // 禁用时清空其他设置
          mapping.longMessage.threshold = undefined;
          mapping.longMessage.appendMessage = undefined;
        }
      } else if (field === 'threshold') {
        const numeric = typeof value === 'number' ? value : parseInt(value, 10);
        mapping.longMessage.threshold = Number.isFinite(numeric) ? numeric : undefined;
      } else if (field === 'appendMessage') {
        mapping.longMessage.appendMessage = value || undefined;
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    // 超长消息配置弹窗相关函数
    let currentLongMessageMappingIndex = -1;
    let currentLongMessageForwardingType = '';

    function openLongMessageConfigModal(mappingIndex, forwardingType) {
      currentLongMessageMappingIndex = mappingIndex;
      currentLongMessageForwardingType = forwardingType;

      const acc = getActiveAccount();

      // 根据转发类型从正确的位置获取映射
      let mapping;
      if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
        mapping = acc.telegramConfig?.mappings?.[mappingIndex];
      } else {
        mapping = acc.mappings[mappingIndex];
      }

      if (!mapping) {
        console.error('Mapping not found:', mappingIndex, forwardingType);
        return;
      }

      const enabledCheckbox = document.getElementById('longMessageEnabled');
      const configSection = document.getElementById('longMessageConfigSection');
      const thresholdInput = document.getElementById('longMessageThreshold');
      const appendTextTextarea = document.getElementById('longMessageAppendText');

      const longMessage = mapping.longMessage || {};

      enabledCheckbox.checked = longMessage.enabled || false;
      thresholdInput.value = longMessage.threshold || '';
      appendTextTextarea.value = longMessage.appendMessage || '';

      toggleLongMessageConfig();

      document.getElementById('longMessageModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    function closeLongMessageConfigModal() {
      document.getElementById('longMessageModal').classList.add('hidden');
      currentLongMessageMappingIndex = -1;
      currentLongMessageForwardingType = '';
    }

    // 通用确认弹窗相关函数
    let confirmActionCallback = null;

    function showConfirmModal(title, message, actionCallback, actionBtnText = '确认', actionBtnClass = 'bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700') {
      document.getElementById('confirmModalTitle').textContent = title;
      document.getElementById('confirmModalMessage').textContent = message;
      document.getElementById('confirmModalActionBtn').textContent = actionBtnText;
      document.getElementById('confirmModalActionBtn').className = `px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white ${actionBtnClass} rounded-lg`;

      confirmActionCallback = actionCallback;
      document.getElementById('confirmModal').classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    function closeConfirmModal() {
      document.getElementById('confirmModal').classList.add('hidden');
      confirmActionCallback = null;
    }

    function executeConfirmAction() {
      if (confirmActionCallback) {
        confirmActionCallback();
      }
      closeConfirmModal();
    }

    function toggleLongMessageConfig() {
      const enabled = document.getElementById('longMessageEnabled').checked;
      const configSection = document.getElementById('longMessageConfigSection');

      if (enabled) {
        configSection.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'pointer-events-none');
      } else {
        configSection.classList.add('opacity-50', 'pointer-events-none');
      }
    }

    function saveLongMessageConfig() {
      if (currentLongMessageMappingIndex === -1) return;

      const enabled = document.getElementById('longMessageEnabled').checked;
      const threshold = parseInt(document.getElementById('longMessageThreshold').value) || 0;
      const appendText = document.getElementById('longMessageAppendText').value;

      updateMappingLongMessage(currentLongMessageMappingIndex, 'enabled', enabled);
      if (enabled) {
        updateMappingLongMessage(currentLongMessageMappingIndex, 'threshold', threshold);
        updateMappingLongMessage(currentLongMessageMappingIndex, 'appendMessage', appendText);
      }

      closeLongMessageConfigModal();
    }

    function updateForwardingUI() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const forwardingType = acc.forwardingType || 'discord-to-discord';
      currentForwardingType = forwardingType; // 更新全局变量
      // 当转发类型改变时，可能需要重置一些相关字段
      if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram') {
        // 确保Discord Token存在
        if (!acc.token) acc.token = '';
        // 初始化Telegram Bot状态
        if (!acc.telegramBotState) acc.telegramBotState = 'idle';
        ensureTelegramConfig(acc);
      } else if (forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
        // 确保Telegram配置存在
        if (!acc.telegramApiId) acc.telegramApiId = '';
        if (!acc.telegramApiHash) acc.telegramApiHash = '';
        // 初始化Telegram Client状态
        if (!acc.telegramClientState) acc.telegramClientState = 'idle';
        ensureTelegramConfig(acc);
      } else if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-feishu') {
        // 确保Discord Token和飞书配置存在
        if (!acc.token) acc.token = '';
        if (!acc.feishuAppId) acc.feishuAppId = '';
        if (!acc.feishuAppSecret) acc.feishuAppSecret = '';
        acc.enableFeishuForward = acc.enableFeishuForward !== true ? true : acc.enableFeishuForward;
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function switchAccount(id) {
      state.activeId = id;
      // 更新当前转发类型为新账号的类型
      const activeAccount = state.accounts.find(a => a.id === id);
      if (activeAccount) {
        currentForwardingType = activeAccount.forwardingType || 'discord-to-discord';
      }
      render();
    }

    // 转发类型切换
    function switchForwardingType(type) {
      currentForwardingType = type;

      // 更新标签页样式
      document.getElementById('discordToDiscordTab').className = type === 'discord-to-discord'
        ? 'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow'
        : 'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition bg-white text-slate-600 border border-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-100';

      document.getElementById('discordToTelegramTab').className = type === 'discord-to-telegram'
        ? 'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow'
        : 'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition bg-white text-slate-600 border border-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-100';

      document.getElementById('telegramToDiscordTab').className = type === 'telegram-to-discord'
        ? 'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow'
        : 'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition bg-white text-slate-600 border border-slate-200 hover:bg-slate-100';

      render();
    }

    function addAccount() {
      const newAcc = {
        id: genId(),
        name: `转发实例${state.accounts.length + 1}`,
        type: 'selfbot',
        token: '',
        proxyUrl: '',
        loginRequested: false,
        loginState: 'idle',
        showSourceIdentity: false,
        forwardingType: 'discord-to-discord', // 添加默认转发类型
        mappings: [],
        blockedKeywords: [],
        excludeKeywords: [],
        replacements: [],
        allowedUsersIds: [],
        mutedUsersIds: [],
        enableTranslation: false,
        translationProvider: 'deepseek',
        translationApiKey: '',
        translationSecret: '',
        deepseekApiKey: '',
        enableBotRelay: false,
        enableDiscordForward: true,
        botRelays: [],
        channelRelayMap: {},
        channelFeishuWebhooks: {},
        enableFeishuForward: false,
        feishuAppId: '',
        feishuAppSecret: '',
        publicBaseUrl: '',
        ignoreSelf: false,
        ignoreBot: false,
         ignoreImages: false,
         ignoreAudio: false,
         ignoreVideo: false,
         ignoreDocuments: false,
         ocrServerUrl: 'http://localhost:9003',
         ocrBlockedKeywords: []
       };
      state.accounts.push(newAcc);
      state.activeId = newAcc.id;
      currentForwardingType = 'discord-to-discord'; // 更新当前转发类型
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function removeAccount() {
      if (state.accounts.length <= 1) {
        showConfirmModal('无法删除', '至少需要保留一个转发实例。', () => {}, '确定', 'bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700');
        return;
      }
      showConfirmModal('删除转发实例', '确定要删除当前转发实例吗？此操作无法撤销。', () => {
        state.accounts = state.accounts.filter(a => a.id !== state.activeId);
        state.activeId = state.accounts[0]?.id || '';
        saveConfig();
        render();
      }, '删除', 'bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700');
    }

    function addMapping() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const forwardingType = acc.forwardingType || currentForwardingType;

      // 根据转发类型决定添加到哪里
      if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
        // Discord→Telegram / Telegram→Discord 转发规则
        ensureTelegramConfig(acc);

        const newMapping = {
          id: genId(),
          sourceChannelId: '',
          targetChannelId: '',
          type: forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? 'telegram-to-discord' : 'discord-to-telegram',
          note: '',
          translate: false,
          translateDirection: 'auto'
        };
        console.log('[DEBUG] 添加新 Telegram 规则:', newMapping.id);

        acc.telegramConfig.mappings.unshift(newMapping);
        console.log('[DEBUG] 当前 telegramConfig.mappings 长度:', acc.telegramConfig.mappings.length);
      } else {
        // Discord→Discord 转发规则
        if (!acc.mappings) acc.mappings = [];

        const newMapping = { id: genId(), sourceChannelId: '', targetWebhookUrl: '', note: '' };
        console.log('[DEBUG] 添加新规则到开头:', newMapping.id);

        acc.mappings.unshift(newMapping);
        console.log('[DEBUG] 当前mappings长度:', acc.mappings.length);
        console.log('[DEBUG] 第一个mapping ID:', acc.mappings[0]?.id);
      }

      pagination.discordPage = 1;
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function goToDiscordPage(page) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const forwardingType = acc.forwardingType || currentForwardingType;
      const mappings = (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord')
        ? (acc.telegramConfig?.mappings || [])
        : (acc.mappings || []);
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(mappings.length / pagination.pageSize) || 1;
      if (page < 1 || page > totalPages) return;
      pagination.discordPage = page;
      render();
    }

    function updateMapping(idx, field, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const forwardingType = acc.forwardingType || currentForwardingType;

      // 根据转发类型决定更新哪个数组
      if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
        // 更新 Telegram 规则
        ensureTelegramConfig(acc);

        if (acc.telegramConfig.mappings[idx]) {
          acc.telegramConfig.mappings[idx][field] = value;
          if (!acc.telegramConfig.mappings[idx].type) {
            acc.telegramConfig.mappings[idx].type = forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord' ? 'telegram-to-discord' : 'discord-to-telegram';
          }
          console.log('[DEBUG] 更新 Telegram 规则:', idx, field, value);
        }
        // 立即保存关键字段
        if (['sourceChannelId', 'targetChannelId', 'note'].includes(field)) {
          saveConfigImmediate();
        } else {
          saveConfig();
        }
      } else {
        // 更新 Discord→Discord 规则
        if (acc.mappings[idx]) {
          const prevSource = acc.mappings[idx].sourceChannelId;
          acc.mappings[idx][field] = value;
          if (field === 'sourceChannelId') {
            if (!acc.channelRelayMap) acc.channelRelayMap = {};
            if (prevSource && acc.channelRelayMap[prevSource]) {
              const relayId = acc.channelRelayMap[prevSource];
              delete acc.channelRelayMap[prevSource];
              if (value) {
                acc.channelRelayMap[String(value)] = relayId;
              }
            }
            if (!acc.channelFeishuWebhooks) acc.channelFeishuWebhooks = {};
            if (prevSource && acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[prevSource]) {
              const feishu = acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[prevSource];
              delete acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[prevSource];
              if (value) {
                acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[String(value)] = feishu;
              }
            }
            if (!acc.channelTranslate) acc.channelTranslate = {};
            if (prevSource && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(acc.channelTranslate, prevSource)) {
              const tr = acc.channelTranslate[prevSource];
              delete acc.channelTranslate[prevSource];
              if (value) {
                acc.channelTranslate[String(value)] = tr;
              }
            }
            if (!acc.channelTranslateDirection) acc.channelTranslateDirection = {};
            if (prevSource && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(acc.channelTranslateDirection, prevSource)) {
              const dir = acc.channelTranslateDirection[prevSource];
              delete acc.channelTranslateDirection[prevSource];
              if (value) {
                acc.channelTranslateDirection[String(value)] = dir;
              }
            }
          }
          if (field === 'translateDirection') {
            if (!acc.channelTranslateDirection) acc.channelTranslateDirection = {};
            const sourceId = acc.mappings[idx].sourceChannelId;
            if (value === 'off') {
              // 关闭翻译时，删除该频道的翻译配置
              if (acc.channelTranslateDirection[sourceId]) {
                delete acc.channelTranslateDirection[sourceId];
              }
              if (acc.channelTranslate && acc.channelTranslate[sourceId]) {
                delete acc.channelTranslate[sourceId];
              }
            } else {
            // 开启翻译时，设置翻译方向
            acc.channelTranslateDirection[sourceId] = value;
            if (!acc.channelTranslate) acc.channelTranslate = {};
            acc.channelTranslate[sourceId] = true;
          }
        }
        saveConfig();
      }
    }
  }

    function removeMapping(idx) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const forwardingType = acc.forwardingType || currentForwardingType;

      // 根据转发类型决定删除哪个数组中的规则
      if (forwardingType === 'discord-to-telegram' || forwardingType === 'telegram-to-discord') {
        // 删除 Telegram 规则
        if (!acc.telegramConfig || !acc.telegramConfig.mappings || idx >= acc.telegramConfig.mappings.length) return;

        acc.telegramConfig.mappings.splice(idx, 1);
        console.log('[DEBUG] 删除 Telegram 规则:', idx);

        // 删除后调整分页
        const { discordPage, pageSize } = pagination;
        const totalPages = Math.ceil(acc.telegramConfig.mappings.length / pageSize) || 1;

        if (discordPage > totalPages) {
          pagination.discordPage = totalPages;
        }

        const currentPageStart = (pagination.discordPage - 1) * pageSize;
        const currentPageEnd = currentPageStart + pageSize;
        const currentPageItems = acc.telegramConfig.mappings.slice(currentPageStart, currentPageEnd);

        if (currentPageItems.length === 0 && pagination.discordPage > 1) {
          pagination.discordPage = 1;
        }
      } else {
        // 删除 Discord→Discord 规则
        if (!acc.mappings || idx >= acc.mappings.length) return;

        const sourceId = acc.mappings[idx]?.sourceChannelId;
        acc.mappings.splice(idx, 1);
        if (sourceId && acc.channelRelayMap && acc.channelRelayMap[sourceId]) {
          delete acc.channelRelayMap[sourceId];
        }

        // 删除后调整分页
        const { discordPage, pageSize } = pagination;
        const totalPages = Math.ceil(acc.mappings.length / pageSize) || 1;

        if (discordPage > totalPages) {
          pagination.discordPage = totalPages;
        }

        const currentPageStart = (pagination.discordPage - 1) * pageSize;
        const currentPageEnd = currentPageStart + pageSize;
        const currentPageItems = acc.mappings.slice(currentPageStart, currentPageEnd);

        if (currentPageItems.length === 0 && pagination.discordPage > 1) {
          pagination.discordPage = 1;
        }
      }

      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateMappingRelay(idx, relayId) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const mapping = acc.mappings?.[idx];
      if (!mapping || !mapping.sourceChannelId) return;
      if (!acc.channelRelayMap) acc.channelRelayMap = {};
      if (relayId) {
        acc.channelRelayMap[mapping.sourceChannelId] = relayId;
      } else {
        delete acc.channelRelayMap[mapping.sourceChannelId];
      }
      saveConfig();
    }

    function goToFeishuPage(page) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(entries.length / pagination.pageSize) || 1;
      if (page < 1 || page > totalPages) return;
      pagination.feishuPage = page;
      render();
    }

    function addFeishuMapping() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.channelFeishuWebhooks) acc.channelFeishuWebhooks = {};
      // 使用时间戳作为key，确保新规则排在前面
      const newKey = 'new_' + Date.now();
      acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[newKey] = { mode: 'webhook', webhookUrl: '' };
      pagination.feishuPage = 1;
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateFeishuSource(idx, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.channelFeishuWebhooks) acc.channelFeishuWebhooks = {};
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const hit = entries[idx];
      if (!hit) return;
      const oldSource = hit.sourceChannelId;
      const webhook = acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[oldSource];
      const notes = acc.channelNotes || {};
      delete acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[oldSource];
      acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[value || ''] = webhook;
      if (notes && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(notes, oldSource)) {
        notes[value || ''] = notes[oldSource];
        if (oldSource !== (value || '')) delete notes[oldSource];
        acc.channelNotes = notes;
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateFeishuWebhookEntry(idx, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.channelFeishuWebhooks) acc.channelFeishuWebhooks = {};
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const hit = entries[idx];
      if (!hit) return;
      const source = hit.sourceChannelId;
      const trimmed = value ? value.trim() : '';
      if (trimmed) {
        acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source] = { mode: 'webhook', webhookUrl: trimmed };
      } else {
        delete acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source];
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateFeishuMode(idx, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.channelFeishuWebhooks) acc.channelFeishuWebhooks = {};
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const hit = entries[idx];
      if (!hit) return;
      const source = hit.sourceChannelId;
      const current = normalizeFeishuTargetValue(acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source]);
      if (value === 'thread') {
        acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source] = {
          mode: 'thread',
          threadId: current.threadId || '',
        };
      } else {
        acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source] = {
          mode: 'webhook',
          webhookUrl: current.webhookUrl || '',
        };
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateFeishuThreadId(idx, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.channelFeishuWebhooks) acc.channelFeishuWebhooks = {};
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const hit = entries[idx];
      if (!hit) return;
      const source = hit.sourceChannelId;
      const trimmed = value ? value.trim() : '';
      if (trimmed) {
        acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source] = {
          mode: 'thread',
          threadId: trimmed,
        };
      } else {
        delete acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source];
      }
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateFeishuNote(idx, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const hit = entries[idx];
      if (!hit) return;
      const source = hit.sourceChannelId;
      if (!acc.channelNotes) acc.channelNotes = {};
      if (value && value.trim()) {
        acc.channelNotes[source] = value.trim();
      } else {
        delete acc.channelNotes[source];
      }
      saveConfig();
    }

    function removeFeishuMapping(idx) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const entries = getFeishuMappings(acc);
      const hit = entries[idx];
      if (!hit) return;

      const source = hit.sourceChannelId;
      delete acc.channelFeishuWebhooks[source];
      if (acc.channelNotes && acc.channelNotes[source] !== undefined) {
        delete acc.channelNotes[source];
      }

      // 删除后调整分页
      const updatedEntries = Object.entries(acc.channelFeishuWebhooks || {});
      const { feishuPage, pageSize } = pagination;
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(updatedEntries.length / pageSize) || 1;

      if (feishuPage > totalPages) {
        // 如果当前页超出范围，跳转到最后一页
        pagination.feishuPage = totalPages;
      }

      // 如果当前页没有内容了，跳转到第一页
      const currentPageStart = (pagination.feishuPage - 1) * pageSize;
      const currentPageEnd = currentPageStart + pageSize;
      const currentPageItems = updatedEntries.slice(currentPageStart, currentPageEnd);

      if (currentPageItems.length === 0 && pagination.feishuPage > 1) {
        pagination.feishuPage = 1;
      }

      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    async function handleKeywordEnter(inputEl, field, isOCR = false) {
      const value = inputEl.value;
      if (!value || !value.trim()) return;

      inputEl.value = '';

      if (isOCR) {
        await addOCRKeyword(field, value);
      } else {
        await addKeyword(field, value);
      }
    }

    async function addKeyword(field, value) {
      if (!value || !value.trim()) return;
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc[field]) acc[field] = [];
      if (!acc[field].includes(value.trim())) {
        acc[field].push(value.trim());
        console.log('[DEBUG] 添加关键词:', value, '当前列表:', acc[field]);
        try {
          await saveConfigImmediate();
          render();
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('[ERROR] 添加关键词失败', e);
          // 回滚
          acc[field] = acc[field].filter(k => k !== value.trim());
          render();
        }
      } else {
        alert('该关键词已存在');
      }
    }

    async function removeKeyword(field, keyword) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const oldValue = [...(acc[field] || [])];
      acc[field] = acc[field].filter(k => k !== keyword);
      console.log('[DEBUG] 删除关键词:', keyword, '剩余列表:', acc[field]);
      try {
        await saveConfigImmediate();
        render();
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] 删除关键词失败', e);
        // 回滚
        acc[field] = oldValue;
        render();
      }
    }

    async function addOCRKeyword(field, value) {
      if (!value.trim()) return;
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc[field]) acc[field] = [];
      if (!acc[field].includes(value.trim())) {
        acc[field].push(value.trim());
        console.log('[DEBUG] 添加OCR关键词:', value, '当前列表:', acc[field]);
        try {
          await saveConfigImmediate();
          render();
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('[ERROR] 添加OCR关键词失败', e);
          // 回滚
          acc[field] = acc[field].filter(k => k !== value.trim());
          render();
        }
      } else {
        alert('该关键词已存在');
      }
    }

    async function loadSessionFile(input) {
      const file = input.files[0];
      if (!file) return;

      // 增加简单的检查，防止误上传二进制文件
      if (file.size > 1024 * 1024) { // 1MB
        alert("文件过大，Session 文件通常很小。请确认上传的是正确的 Session 文件。");
        return;
      }

      const acc = getActiveAccount();

      try {
        const form = new FormData();
        form.append('accountId', acc.id);
        form.append('file', file, file.name);

        const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/client/session-file', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: form
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (!res.ok) {
          throw new Error(data?.error || data?.message || `上传失败(${res.status})`);
        }

        acc.telegramSessionPath = data.sessionPath || '';
        acc.telegramSessionString = '';
        acc.sessionType = 'file';
        saveConfig();
        render();
        alert("Session 文件已上传并保存。");
      } catch (e) {
        alert("Session 文件上传失败: " + (e?.message || e));
      }
    }

    function switchSessionType(type) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      acc.sessionType = type;
      updateField('sessionType', type);

      // 更新tab样式
      const fileTab = document.getElementById('sessionFileTab');
      const stringTab = document.getElementById('sessionStringTab');
      const fileContent = document.getElementById('sessionFileContent');
      const stringContent = document.getElementById('sessionStringContent');

      if (type === 'file') {
        fileTab.className = 'flex-1 py-2 px-3 text-sm font-medium text-center bg-white text-indigo-600 border-b-2 border-indigo-600';
        stringTab.className = 'flex-1 py-2 px-3 text-sm font-medium text-center text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-700';
        fileContent.classList.remove('hidden');
        stringContent.classList.add('hidden');
      } else {
        stringTab.className = 'flex-1 py-2 px-3 text-sm font-medium text-center bg-white text-indigo-600 border-b-2 border-indigo-600';
        fileTab.className = 'flex-1 py-2 px-3 text-sm font-medium text-center text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-700';
        stringContent.classList.remove('hidden');
        fileContent.classList.add('hidden');
      }
    }

    async function removeOCRKeyword(field, keyword) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const oldValue = [...(acc[field] || [])];
      acc[field] = acc[field].filter(k => k !== keyword);
      console.log('[DEBUG] 删除OCR关键词:', keyword, '剩余列表:', acc[field]);
      try {
        await saveConfigImmediate();
        render();
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[ERROR] 删除OCR关键词失败', e);
        // 回滚
        acc[field] = oldValue;
        render();
      }
    }

    function addReplacement() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.replacements) acc.replacements = [];
      acc.replacements.push({ from: '', to: '' });
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateReplacement(idx, field, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.replacements[idx]) {
        acc.replacements[idx][field] = value;
        saveConfig();
      }
    }

    function removeReplacement(idx) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      acc.replacements.splice(idx, 1);
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function goToBotRelayPage(page) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      const relays = acc.botRelays || [];
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(relays.length / pagination.pageSize) || 1;
      if (page < 1 || page > totalPages) return;
      pagination.botRelayPage = page;
      render();
    }

    function addBotRelay() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.botRelays) acc.botRelays = [];
      // 添加到数组开头，这样会显示在第一页第一行
      acc.botRelays.unshift({ id: genId(), name: `中转机器人${acc.botRelays.length + 1}`, token: '', loginState: 'idle', loginMessage: '' });
      pagination.botRelayPage = 1;
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function updateBotRelay(idx, field, value) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.botRelays || !acc.botRelays[idx]) return;
      acc.botRelays[idx][field] = value;
      saveConfig();
    }

    function removeBotRelay(idx) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!acc.botRelays || idx >= acc.botRelays.length) return;

      const removed = acc.botRelays[idx];
      acc.botRelays.splice(idx, 1);
      // 清理映射中使用该机器人的绑定
      if (removed?.id && acc.channelRelayMap) {
        Object.keys(acc.channelRelayMap).forEach((k) => {
          if (acc.channelRelayMap[k] === removed.id) {
            delete acc.channelRelayMap[k];
          }
        });
      }

      // 删除后调整分页，确保不会超出页面范围
      const { botRelayPage, pageSize } = pagination;
      const totalPages = Math.ceil(acc.botRelays.length / pageSize) || 1;
      if (botRelayPage > totalPages) {
        pagination.botRelayPage = totalPages;
      }
      // 如果当前页变空，且不是第一页，则跳转到第一页
      const currentPageStart = (pagination.botRelayPage - 1) * pageSize;
      const currentPageEnd = currentPageStart + pageSize;
      const currentPageItems = acc.botRelays.slice(currentPageStart, currentPageEnd);
      if (currentPageItems.length === 0 && pagination.botRelayPage > 1) {
        pagination.botRelayPage = 1;
      }

      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    async function requestRelayLogin(relayId) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!relayId) return;
      const current = (acc.botRelays || []).find(r => r.id === relayId);
      if (current && (current.loginState === 'pending' || current.loginState === 'online')) return;
      // 本地先置为 pending
      acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) =>
        r.id === relayId ? { ...r, loginState: 'pending', loginMessage: '正在登录 Token...' } : r
      );
      render();
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/account/action', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id, action: 'relayLogin', relayIds: [relayId] })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data?.results) {
          acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) => {
            const hit = data.results[r.id];
            return hit ? { ...r, loginState: hit.loginState, loginMessage: hit.loginMessage } : r;
          });
          saveConfig();
        } else if (!res.ok) {
          acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) =>
            r.id === relayId ? { ...r, loginState: 'error', loginMessage: data?.error || `登录失败(${res.status})` } : r
          );
          saveConfig();
        }
        render();
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('relay login failed', e);
        acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) =>
          r.id === relayId ? { ...r, loginState: 'error', loginMessage: '请求失败' } : r
        );
        saveConfig();
        render();
      }
    }

    async function requestRelayLoginAll() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      // 如果全部都在 pending/online 则跳过
      const canLogin = (acc.botRelays || []).some(r => r.loginState !== 'pending' && r.loginState !== 'online');
      if (!canLogin) return;
      // 本地先置为 pending
      acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) => ({ ...r, loginState: 'pending', loginMessage: '正在登录 Token...' }));
      render();
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/account/action', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id, action: 'relayLogin' })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data?.results) {
          acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) => {
            const hit = data.results[r.id];
            return hit ? { ...r, loginState: hit.loginState, loginMessage: hit.loginMessage } : r;
          });
          saveConfig();
        } else if (!res.ok) {
          acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) => ({
            ...r,
            loginState: 'error',
            loginMessage: data?.error || `登录失败(${res.status})`,
          }));
          saveConfig();
        }
        render();
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('relay login all failed', e);
        acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) => ({ ...r, loginState: 'error', loginMessage: '请求失败' }));
        saveConfig();
        render();
      }
    }

    function requestRelayStop(relayId) {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (!relayId) return;
      acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) =>
        r.id === relayId ? { ...r, loginState: 'idle', loginMessage: '已停止' } : r
      );
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    function requestRelayStopAll() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      acc.botRelays = (acc.botRelays || []).map((r) => ({ ...r, loginState: 'idle', loginMessage: '已停止' }));
      saveConfig();
      render();
    }

    async function requestLogin() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.loginState === 'online' || acc.loginState === 'pending') return;
      
      acc.loginState = 'pending';
      acc.loginMessage = '正在登录...';
      render();

      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/account/action', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id, action: 'login' })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (!res.ok && data.loginState === 'online') {
          acc.loginState = 'online';
          acc.loginMessage = '已登录';
        }
      } catch (e) {
        acc.loginState = 'idle';
        acc.loginMessage = '登录请求失败';
      }
      render();
    }

    async function requestStop() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.loginState === 'pending' || (acc.loginState !== 'online' && acc.loginState !== 'error')) return;
      
      acc.loginState = 'idle';
      acc.loginMessage = '正在停止...';
      render();

      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/account/action', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id, action: 'stop' })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          acc.loginState = data.loginState || 'idle';
          acc.loginMessage = data.loginMessage || '已停止';
        }
      } catch (e) {
        acc.loginState = acc.loginState || 'idle';
        acc.loginMessage = '停止请求失败';
      }
      render();
    }

    // 自动检查 Telegram Bot 连接状态（页面加载时调用）
    async function autoCheckTelegramBotStatus() {
      for (const acc of state.accounts) {
        // 检查是否有 Token 和转发规则
        if (acc.telegramBotToken && acc.telegramBotToken.trim() !== '') {
          const telegramMappings = acc.telegramConfig?.mappings || [];
          const hasDiscordToTelegramMapping = telegramMappings.some(m => m.type === 'discord-to-telegram');

          // 只有配置了转发规则才自动检查状态
          if (!hasDiscordToTelegramMapping) {
            acc.telegramBotState = 'idle';
            continue;
          }

          try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/bot/connect', {
              method: 'POST',
              headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
              body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id })
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            acc.telegramBotState = data.state || (res.ok ? 'online' : 'error');
            if (data.message) {
              acc.telegramBotMessage = data.message;
            }
          } catch (e) {
            acc.telegramBotState = 'error';
            acc.telegramBotMessage = '连接检查失败';
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // 自动检查 Telegram Client 连接状态（页面加载时调用）
    async function autoCheckTelegramClientStatus() {
      for (const acc of state.accounts) {
        const telegramMappings = acc.telegramConfig?.mappings || [];
        const hasTelegramToDiscordMapping = telegramMappings.some(m => m.type === 'telegram-to-discord');
        if (!hasTelegramToDiscordMapping) {
          acc.telegramClientState = 'idle';
          continue;
        }

        const hasApiId = acc.telegramApiId !== undefined && String(acc.telegramApiId).trim() !== '';
        const hasApiHash = acc.telegramApiHash && String(acc.telegramApiHash).trim();
        const hasSession = (acc.telegramSessionString && acc.telegramSessionString.trim())
          || (acc.telegramSessionPath && acc.telegramSessionPath.trim());
        if (!hasApiId || !hasApiHash || !hasSession) {
          continue;
        }

        try {
          const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/client/status', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id })
          });
          const data = await res.json();
          acc.telegramClientState = data.state || (res.ok ? 'online' : 'error');
          acc.telegramClientMessage = data.message || acc.telegramClientMessage || '';
        } catch (e) {
          acc.telegramClientState = acc.telegramClientState || 'idle';
          acc.telegramClientMessage = '状态获取失败';
        }
      }
    }

    // Telegram Bot 连接函数
    async function connectTelegramBot() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.telegramBotState === 'online' || acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting') return;

      // 验证是否配置了转发规则
      const telegramMappings = acc.telegramConfig?.mappings || [];
      const hasDiscordToTelegramMapping = telegramMappings.some(m => m.type === 'discord-to-telegram');

      if (!hasDiscordToTelegramMapping) {
        acc.telegramBotState = 'error';
        acc.telegramBotMessage = '未配置 Discord → Telegram 转发规则，无法启动';
        render();
        return;
      }

      acc.telegramBotState = 'connecting';
      acc.telegramBotMessage = '正在连接Telegram Bot...';
      render();

      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/bot/connect', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          acc.telegramBotState = data.state || 'online';
          acc.telegramBotMessage = data.message || '连接成功';
        } else {
          acc.telegramBotState = 'error';
          acc.telegramBotMessage = data.message || '连接失败';
        }
      } catch (e) {
        acc.telegramBotState = 'error';
        acc.telegramBotMessage = '连接请求失败';
      }
      render();
    }

    // Telegram Bot 断开函数
    async function disconnectTelegramBot() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.telegramBotState === 'connecting' || (acc.telegramBotState !== 'online' && acc.telegramBotState !== 'error')) return;

      acc.telegramBotState = 'idle';
      acc.telegramBotMessage = '正在断开...';
      render();

      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/bot/disconnect', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          acc.telegramBotState = data.state || 'idle';
          acc.telegramBotMessage = data.message || '已断开';
        }
      } catch (e) {
        acc.telegramBotState = acc.telegramBotState || 'idle';
        acc.telegramBotMessage = '断开请求失败';
      }
      render();
    }

    // Telegram Client 连接函数
    async function connectTelegramClient() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.telegramClientState === 'online' || acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting') return;

      const hasApiId = acc.telegramApiId !== undefined && String(acc.telegramApiId).trim() !== '';
      const hasApiHash = acc.telegramApiHash && String(acc.telegramApiHash).trim();
      const hasSession = (acc.telegramSessionString && acc.telegramSessionString.trim())
        || (acc.telegramSessionPath && acc.telegramSessionPath.trim());
      if (!hasApiId || !hasApiHash) {
        acc.telegramClientState = 'error';
        acc.telegramClientMessage = '缺少 Telegram API ID 或 API Hash';
        render();
        return;
      }
      if (!hasSession) {
        acc.telegramClientState = 'error';
        acc.telegramClientMessage = '缺少 Telegram Session（文件或字符串）';
        render();
        return;
      }

      acc.telegramClientState = 'connecting';
      acc.telegramClientMessage = '正在连接Telegram Client...';
      render();

      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/client/connect', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          acc.telegramClientState = data.state || 'online';
          acc.telegramClientMessage = data.message || '连接成功';
        } else {
          acc.telegramClientState = 'error';
          acc.telegramClientMessage = data.message || '连接失败';
        }
      } catch (e) {
        acc.telegramClientState = 'error';
        acc.telegramClientMessage = '连接请求失败';
      }
      render();
    }

    // Telegram Client 断开函数
    async function disconnectTelegramClient() {
      const acc = getActiveAccount();
      if (acc.telegramClientState === 'connecting' || (acc.telegramClientState !== 'online' && acc.telegramClientState !== 'error')) return;

      acc.telegramClientState = 'idle';
      acc.telegramClientMessage = '正在断开...';
      render();

      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/telegram/client/disconnect', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ accountId: acc.id })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          acc.telegramClientState = data.state || 'idle';
          acc.telegramClientMessage = data.message || '已断开';
        }
      } catch (e) {
        acc.telegramClientState = acc.telegramClientState || 'idle';
        acc.telegramClientMessage = '断开请求失败';
      }
      render();
    }

    function showHelp() {
      document.getElementById('helpPanel').classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    function hideHelp() {
      document.getElementById('helpPanel').classList.add('hidden');
    }

    async function exportConfig() {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/config');
        const data = await res.json();
        const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = url;
        a.download = `discord-forwarder-config-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace(/:/g, '-')}.json`;
        a.click();
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
      } catch (e) {
        alert('导出失败: ' + e.message);
      }
    }

    // 状态轮询
    function startStatusPolling() {
      setInterval(async () => {
        try {
          const res = await fetch('/api/config');
          const data = await res.json();
          if (Array.isArray(data?.accounts)) {
            const hasChange = data.accounts.some((ra, idx) => {
              const la = state.accounts[idx];
              if (!la) return false;
              return (
                ra.loginState !== la.loginState || 
                ra.loginMessage !== la.loginMessage
              );
            });
            if (hasChange) {
              state.accounts.forEach((acc, idx) => {
                const remote = data.accounts[idx];
                if (remote && acc.id === remote.id) {
                  if (acc.loginState !== 'pending' || remote.loginState !== 'idle') {
                    acc.loginState = remote.loginState || acc.loginState;
                    acc.loginMessage = remote.loginMessage || acc.loginMessage;
                  }
                }
              });
              if (isFormElementActive()) {
                pendingStatusRender = true;
              } else {
                render();
              }
            }
          }
        } catch (e) {
          // 忽略轮询错误
        }
      }, 2000);
    }

    // 启动
    init();
  </script>

  <!-- Telegram超长消息处理配置弹窗 -->
  <div id="longMessageModal" class="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 hidden z-50">
    <div class="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-4">
      <div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-xl max-w-md w-full">
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between p-6 border-b border-slate-200">
          <h3 class="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-800">超长消息处理配置</h3>
          <button onclick="closeLongMessageConfigModal()" class="text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-600">
            <svg class="w-6 h-6" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
              <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12"></path>
            </svg>
          </button>
        </div>
        <div class="p-6 space-y-4">

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>OCR关键词调试</title>
    <style>
        body { font-family: sans-serif; padding: 20px; }
        .keyword { background: #fef3c7; padding: 4px 8px; margin: 4px; border-radius: 4px; display: inline-block; }
        .error { color: red; }
        .success { color: green; }
        .log { font-family: monospace; font-size: 12px; background: #f3f4f6; padding: 10px; margin-top: 20px; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <h2>OCR关键词测试（带调试）</h2>
    
    <div>
        <label>关键词列表：</label>
        <div id="keywordList"></div>
    </div>
    
    <div style="margin: 20px 0;">
        <input type="text" id="keywordInput" placeholder="输入关键词后按回车" style="padding: 8px; width: 300px;">
        <button onclick="simulateAdd()" style="padding: 8px 16px;">模拟添加</button>
        <button onclick="simulateRefresh()" style="padding: 8px 16px;">模拟刷新</button>
    </div>
    
    <div id="log" class="log"></div>
    
    <script>
        let keywords = [];
        let logContainer = document.getElementById('log');
        
        function log(msg, type = 'info') {
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.textContent = `[${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${msg}`;
            div.className = type;
            logContainer.appendChild(div);
            logContainer.scrollTop = logContainer.scrollHeight;
            console.log(msg);
        }
        
        function render() {
            const list = document.getElementById('keywordList');
            list.innerHTML = keywords.map(k => 
                `<span class="keyword">${k} <button onclick="removeKeyword('${k}')">×</button></span>`
            ).join('');
            log('渲染完成，关键词数量: ' + keywords.length);
        }
        
        async function addKeyword(value) {
            if (!value.trim()) {
                log('关键词为空，跳过', 'error');
                return;
            }
            if (keywords.includes(value.trim())) {
                log('关键词已存在: ' + value, 'error');
                alert('该关键词已存在');
                return;
            }
            log('开始添加关键词: ' + value);
            keywords.push(value.trim());
            render();
            
            log('模拟保存到服务器...', 'info');
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 模拟网络延迟
            log('保存完成！', 'success');
        }
        
        function removeKeyword(keyword) {
            log('删除关键词: ' + keyword);
            keywords = keywords.filter(k => k !== keyword);
            render();
        }
        
        async function simulateAdd() {
            const input = document.getElementById('keywordInput');
            const value = input.value.trim();
            if (!value) {
                alert('请输入关键词');
                return;
            }
            input.value = ''; // 立即清空输入框
            try {
                await addKeyword(value);
            } catch (e) {
                log('添加失败: ' + e, 'error');
            }
        }
        
        function simulateRefresh() {
            log('模拟页面刷新...');
            keywords = []; // 清空内存中的数据
            log('模拟从服务器加载: []', 'info');
            render(); // 重新渲染（会显示空列表）
        }
        
        document.getElementById('keywordInput').addEventListener('keydown', async (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                const input = e.target;
                const value = input.value;
                input.value = ''; // 立即清空
                log('回车键触发，输入框已清空: ' + value);
                try {
                    await addKeyword(value);
                } catch (err) {
                    log('添加失败: ' + err, 'error');
                }
            }
        });
        
        render();
        log('初始化完成');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
代码收集脚本
将项目中的所有有效代码文件收集到一个txt文件中
"""

import os
import sys
from pathlib import Path

# 要收集的文件扩展名
EXTENSIONS = {
    '.py', '.ts', '.tsx', '.js', '.jsx',
    '.json', '.md', '.txt', '.yml', '.yaml',
    '.sh', '.bash', '.css', '.scss', '.html'
}

# 要排除的目录
EXCLUDE_DIRS = {
    'node_modules', 'venv', 'ui', '.git',
    'dist', 'dist-bot', 'build', '__pycache__',
    '.next', '.cache', 'logs', '.data',
    'coverage', 'tmp', 'temp'
}

# 要排除的文件
EXCLUDE_FILES = {
    'package-lock.json', 'pnpm-lock.yaml',
    'yarn.lock', '.DS_Store'
}

def should_exclude_path(path: Path, root: Path) -> bool:
    """检查路径是否应该被排除"""
    # 检查路径中是否包含排除的目录
    parts = path.relative_to(root).parts
    for part in parts:
        if part in EXCLUDE_DIRS:
            return True

    # 检查文件名是否在排除列表中
    if path.name in EXCLUDE_FILES:
        return True

    return False

def collect_code_files(root_dir: str, output_file: str):
    """收集所有代码文件到输出文件"""
    root = Path(root_dir).resolve()
    output = Path(output_file).resolve()

    print(f"正在扫描目录: {root}")
    print(f"输出文件: {output}")
    print(f"排除目录: {', '.join(EXCLUDE_DIRS)}")
    print("-" * 60)

    collected_files = []

    # 遍历所有文件
    for file_path in root.rglob('*'):
        # 跳过目录
        if file_path.is_dir():
            continue

        # 跳过输出文件本身
        if file_path == output:
            continue

        # 检查是否应该排除
        if should_exclude_path(file_path, root):
            continue

        # 检查文件扩展名
        if file_path.suffix not in EXTENSIONS:
            continue

        collected_files.append(file_path)

    print(f"找到 {len(collected_files)} 个文件")
    print("-" * 60)

    # 写入输出文件
    with open(output, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(f"代码收集 - {root.name}\n")
        f.write(f"总文件数: {len(collected_files)}\n")
        f.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")

        for i, file_path in enumerate(sorted(collected_files), 1):
            rel_path = file_path.relative_to(root)
            print(f"[{i}/{len(collected_files)}] {rel_path}")

            f.write("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n")
            f.write(f"文件: {rel_path}\n")
            f.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")

            try:
                content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
                f.write(content)
                f.write("\n\n")
            except Exception as e:
                f.write(f"[错误: 无法读取文件 - {e}]\n\n")
                print(f"  ⚠️  无法读取: {e}")

    print("-" * 60)
    print(f"✅ 完成！代码已保存到: {output}")
    print(f"📊 总共收集了 {len(collected_files)} 个文件")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    # 默认参数
    root_dir = os.getcwd()
    output_file = 'collected_code.txt'

    # 解析命令行参数
    if len(sys.argv) > 1:
        root_dir = sys.argv[1]
    if len(sys.argv) > 2:
        output_file = sys.argv[2]

    collect_code_files(root_dir, output_file)

#!/usr/bin/env node

/**
 * 后端统一启动脚本
 * 自动启动：Bot + OCR 服务器 + Telegram Bridge（由 Bot 自动管理）
 */

const { spawn, execSync } = require('child_process');
const path = require('path');
const fs = require('fs');

const processes = [];
let isShuttingDown = false;

// 颜色输出
const colors = {
  reset: '\x1b[0m',
  bright: '\x1b[1m',
  green: '\x1b[32m',
  yellow: '\x1b[33m',
  blue: '\x1b[34m',
  red: '\x1b[31m',
  cyan: '\x1b[36m',
};

function log(prefix, message, color = colors.reset) {
  const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('zh-CN', { hour12: false });
  console.log(`${color}[${timestamp}] [${prefix}]${colors.reset} ${message}`);
}

// 优雅退出处理
function gracefulShutdown(signal) {
  if (isShuttingDown) return;
  isShuttingDown = true;

  log('SHUTDOWN', `收到 ${signal} 信号，正在关闭所有服务...`, colors.yellow);

  processes.forEach((proc, index) => {
    if (proc && !proc.killed) {
      log('SHUTDOWN', `正在停止进程 ${index + 1}...`, colors.yellow);
      proc.kill('SIGTERM');
    }
  });

  setTimeout(() => {
    log('SHUTDOWN', '所有服务已关闭', colors.green);
    process.exit(0);
  }, 2000);
}

process.on('SIGINT', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGINT'));
process.on('SIGTERM', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGTERM'));

// 检查并清理端口
function killProcessOnPort(port) {
  try {
    const result = execSync(`lsof -ti :${port}`, { encoding: 'utf8' }).trim();
    if (result) {
      const pids = result.split('\n').filter(pid => pid);
      pids.forEach(pid => {
        try {
          log('CLEANUP', `正在停止占用端口 ${port} 的进程 (PID: ${pid})...`, colors.yellow);
          execSync(`kill -9 ${pid}`);
          log('CLEANUP', `进程 ${pid} 已停止`, colors.green);
        } catch (e) {
          // 进程可能已经停止
        }
      });
      return true;
    }
  } catch (e) {
    // 端口未被占用
  }
  return false;
}

// 主启动函数
async function startBackend() {
  log('STARTUP', '开始启动后端服务...', colors.bright + colors.cyan);

  // 步骤 1: 编译 Bot
  log('BUILD', '正在编译 Bot...', colors.blue);
  try {
    execSync('pnpm build:bot', { stdio: 'inherit', cwd: path.resolve(__dirname, '..') });
    log('BUILD', 'Bot 编译完成 ✓', colors.green);
  } catch (error) {
    log('BUILD', 'Bot 编译失败 ✗', colors.red);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  // 步骤 2: 启动 OCR 服务器
  log('OCR', '正在启动 OCR 服务器...', colors.blue);

  // 清理端口 9003
  killProcessOnPort(9003);

  const ocrServer = spawn('node', ['paddle_ocr_server.js'], {
    cwd: path.resolve(__dirname, '..'),
    stdio: ['ignore', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
  });

  processes.push(ocrServer);

  ocrServer.stdout.on('data', (data) => {
    log('OCR', data.toString().trim(), colors.cyan);
  });

  ocrServer.stderr.on('data', (data) => {
    log('OCR', data.toString().trim(), colors.yellow);
  });

  ocrServer.on('exit', (code) => {
    if (!isShuttingDown) {
      log('OCR', `OCR 服务器退出，代码: ${code}`, colors.red);
    }
  });

  // 等待 OCR 服务器启动
  await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
  log('OCR', 'OCR 服务器已启动 ✓', colors.green);

  // 步骤 3: 启动 Bot（会自动启动 Telegram Bridge）
  log('BOT', '正在启动 Bot...', colors.blue);
  const bot = spawn('node', ['dist-bot/index.js'], {
    cwd: path.resolve(__dirname, '..'),
    stdio: ['ignore', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
  });

  processes.push(bot);

  bot.stdout.on('data', (data) => {
    log('BOT', data.toString().trim(), colors.green);
  });

  bot.stderr.on('data', (data) => {
    log('BOT', data.toString().trim(), colors.yellow);
  });

  bot.on('exit', (code) => {
    if (!isShuttingDown) {
      log('BOT', `Bot 退出，代码: ${code}`, colors.red);
      gracefulShutdown('BOT_EXIT');
    }
  });

  log('STARTUP', '所有后端服务已启动 ✓', colors.bright + colors.green);
  log('INFO', 'Bot 会自动管理 Telegram Bridge 进程', colors.cyan);
  log('INFO', '按 Ctrl+C 停止所有服务', colors.cyan);
}

// 启动
startBackend().catch((error) => {
  log('ERROR', error.message, colors.red);
  process.exit(1);
});

文件: src/bot.ts
